In our previous research, we have isolated a chlortetracycline degrading strain- Pseudomonas putida. This project will study the chlortetracycline degradation kinetics of this strain and the factors influencing its degradation capacity. We will try to identify the degradation products and elucidate the degradation pathway. Furthermore, the regulatory role of a common clay mineral, kaolinite in the degradation ability of Pseudomonas putida will be determined and extensive analysis of the interactive mode among kaolinite, chlortetracycline and the bacteria strain will be carried out. To get insight into the molecular mechanism underlying the regulation of bacterial degradation by kaolinite, the transcription response of the Pseudomonas putida strain to chlortetracycline with or without the presence of kaolinite will be investigated through RNA-seq. The project results will help us better elucidate the transfer and transformation process of antibiotics in the environment and gain a better understanding of the profound interaction between clay minerals and microbes."	
硒化物微生物矿化亚微观过程及影响因素研究	41703073	生物地球化学 ( D0312 )	袁永强	副研究员	中山大学	25.00万元	青年科学基金项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2020 年 12 月 31 日	生物矿化；硒化物；亚微观过程；影响因素	Biomineralization;Selenide;Submicroscopic process; Influence factor 	本项目针对细菌化石胞内铜硒化物不明成因，在元素硒生物矿化基础上，通过模拟自然环境，开展Cu2+胁迫下细菌Bacillus licheniformis与硒氧离子相互作用下的生物矿化研究。通过实时高分辨成像和X-射线吸收精细结构谱分析，阐明铜硒化物纳米颗粒的亚微观生长过程，确定其生物矿物种类并验证其生物成因；通过生物矿化过程中细菌细胞结构及相关细胞组分、蛋白质特异表达上的实时变化等分析，明晰生物大分子在硒化物纳米颗粒核化与组装中的作用；通过纳米颗粒在不同Cu2+浓度梯度下尺寸与形貌变化，厘清Cu2+对硒生物矿化中纳米矿物颗粒形成的影响，以期从亚微观和分子水平揭示铜硒化物生物矿化的过程及主要影响因素。本研究有助于深化对生物诱导早期纳米成矿过程的认识，也可为硒及共存重金属污染物的生物去除提供理论依据和数据支持，同时，对于丰富硒的生物地球化学循环理论和实际生产应用均具有重要理论指导意义。	"In view of the unknown genesis of intracellular copper selenide in a bacterial fossil, this project will study copper selenide biomineralization through simulation experiment in laboratory, basing on elemental Se biomineralization induced by Bacillus licheniformis SeRB-1. We mainly intend to: (1) reveal submicroscopic processes of nano-biomineral formation intracellularly and extracellularly at early, middle and late mineralization periods, and exhibit biomineral types and verify biogenesis of copper selenide, using real-time high resolution imaging and X- ray absorption fine structure spectrum analysis; (2) illustrate roles of macromolecules in selenide nano-particle nucleation and assembly, through real-time analysis of changes of cell structure, specific cell components and protein specific expression related to biomineralization during interaction between bacteria and minerals; (3) clarify the effect of Cu2+ on selenide nano-particle formation and growth, by real-time imaging of selenide nanoparticles in size and morphology under different Cu2+concentration gradient. Finally, we expect to reveal the processes of nano-mineral formation and main influence factor of selenide biomineralization from mesoscopic and molecular perspectives. This project will deepen understanding of biological induced mineralization of selenide nano-particles in the early stage, but also provide theoretical basis and data support for bioremediation of selenium and its coexistence heavy metal pollutant, e.g., Cu, meanwhile, it is significant for enriching biogeochemical cycle theory of Se and its practical production and application."	
外源有机物质提升典型旱作土壤有机质的微生物介导机制研究	41730753	土壤生物学 ( D070104 )	丁维新	研究员	中国科学院南京土壤研究所	321.00万元	重点项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2022 年 12 月 31 日	土壤微生物群落结构；土壤微生物功能；土壤有机质；团聚体；13C示踪技术	soil microbial community structure;soil microbial function;soil organic matter;soil aggregates;13C tracing	我国土壤有机质含量较低，已成为高产作物品种潜力发挥和水肥高效利用的主要限制因素。然而土壤有机质如何转化，外源有机物质如何有机质化并在土壤中累积，机制尚不清楚。项目拟选取长期定位试验土壤，利用团聚体分级、核磁共振等技术，研究粉粘粒组分中有机质累积特征与团聚体的关系，解析团聚体形成的关键控制因素；采用高通量测序、CT等技术，研究土壤孔隙等性质、微生物群落特点，阐明土壤肥力梯度上微生物群落演替规律及其与有机质和团聚体的耦联关系；建立13C-有机物质微宇宙和微区试验，利用DNA-SIP等技术，研究有机物质13C转化的功能微生物群落和活性，阐明微生物的接力利用机制和相对贡献；利用生物标志物、nanoSIMS等技术，研究有机物质13C在不同土壤中的分解速率、代谢产物来源和在团聚体中分配过程及其与微生物的阻隔关系，揭示有机物质提升土壤有机质的效应及机制，阐明有机质累积规律，为土壤有机质调控提供理论依据。	"The concentration of soil organic carbon in Chinese arable soils is rather low compared with those in USA and European countries, which considerably suppresses the increase of crop yields due to insufficient supply of nutrients and water and lower fertilizer nitrogen use efficiency. Up to date, however, the process of organic carbon accumulation in soils is not well understood, which in turn limits the development of effective practices for improving soil fertility. In the present study, soil samples from three long-term field experiments where organic manure and inorganic fertilizer have been applied will be collected at the Yingtan, Fengqiu and Hailun Agro-ecological experimental stations and then separated into different size aggregates through wet-sieving. The concentration and components of organic matter will be measured in the silt plus clay fraction to understand the accumulation processes of organic matter and its relation to aggregation. The components, molecular structure, stability and sources of organic matter in different size aggregates will also be analyzed using the chemical method and nuclear magnetic resonance technique to understand the distribution and regulation of organic carbon among aggregates. The community structure of microorganisms in soils and aggregates will be determined using the macro genomics, and its relation to organic carbon concentration in soil and aggregates will be evaluated. The relationship between microbial community structure and soil porosity or oxygen diffusion rate will be elucidated. The laboratory incubation with addition of 13C-labelled cellulose to long-term field experimental soils and field experiment with 13C-labelled wheat straw at the Yingtan, Fengqiu and Hailun Agro-ecological experimental stations will be set up. The transformation process of 13C in soils by microorganisms will be monitored by the 13C nucleic acid probe and distribution of 13C in aggregates will be measured to evaluate the influence of soils with different organic carbon concentrations on the residual rate of exogenous organic carbon and the kind of functional microorganisms coupling to decomposition of exogenous organic material. The decomposition rate of added organic material in soils at different regions, and the sources and allocation process of newly formed organic matter in aggregates will be examined. The objective of this study is to understand the accumulation processes of organic carbon and how microorganisms transform exogenous organic material into soil organic matter. Based on this study, effective practices for increasing organic matter in upland soils will be suggested according to soil characteristics especially components of native organic matter."	
耐铊微生物菌株对Tl(I)/Tl(III)形态转化机制研究	41763010	生物地球化学 ( D0312 )	孙嘉龙	研究员	贵州理工学院	37.00万元	地区科学基金项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2021 年 12 月 31 日	铊；耐铊微生物；形态转化；转录组；生物信息学	Thallium;Tl-tolerant microbial groups;Speciation transformation;Transcriptome;Bioinformatics	铊是典型毒害重金属元素，在自然界有两种形态：Tl(I)和Tl(III)，两者生物毒性存在巨大差异，有研究表明两者在微生物作用下可发生转化，但相关作用机理研究较少。在前期工作基础上，本项目以耐铊菌株作用下Tl(I)/Tl(III)的形态转化特征及机制为研究目标，a) 利用微柱分离法和ICP-MS查明培养介质中Tl(I)/Tl(III)含量变化特征，b) 构建氧化还原动力学曲线，考察主控因子对Tl(I)/Tl(III)组成变化特征的影响，c) 应用XANES技术分析细胞内Tl(I)/Tl(III)的分布特征，d) 基于转录组技术阐明影响形态铊转化过程的相关功能蛋白（酶），应用生物信息学解析其影响机制。通过本项目研究，将组建对Tl(I)/Tl(III)具有氧化或还原性的功能性菌群，获取一批丰富的生物地球化学数据，将丰富铊的表生生物地球化学循环的认识，还将为铊污染地区的污染防治等提供科学依据。	"Thallium (Tl) is a severe toxicity heavy metal, which has two chemical speciatons such as Tl(I) and Tl(III). However, the toxicity varies greatly from each speciation and some researchers found that they could transform from each other by the specific microbes. However, little is known on the mechnissm of Tl(I) /Tl(III) transformation. It’s of significant importance to affect the specaiton transformation by means of possible ways including microbiological way. In this proposal, the effect of Tl-tolerant strains on the the specaiton transformation will be studied based on the previous work. The concentrations of Tl(I) and Tl(III) in the liquid substrate added Tl-tolerant strains will be characterized by microcolumn separation with ICP-MS. Besides, the kinetics of Tl(I)/Tl(III) will also be investigated under the different conditions. By using XANES technology, the concentration variations of Tl(I) and Tl(III) in the sub-cellular organelles will be examined. Moreover, the different expression genes will indicate that some kind of metabolisms, even the proteins and enzyme, may be employed to promote the redox activities based on the transcriptome and bioinformatics analysis. Through all these results, the underlying mechanism of Tl-tolerant strains on the Tl speciaton transformation will be revealed. This will shed lights on the the micro-remediation Tl-contaminated soil."	
北方泥炭地不同发育阶段铁碳结合特征及其微生物驱动机制	41771120	综合自然地理学 ( D010107 )	姜明	研究员	中国科学院东北地理与农业生态研究所	70.00万元	面上项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2021 年 12 月 31 日	泥炭地；发育阶段；铁；有机碳；微生物驱动	Peatlands;Development stage;Iron;Organic carbon;Microbial regulation	泥炭地是全球重要的碳库，对全球气候变化极为敏感；独特的氧化还原交替过程使其成为铁、碳、氮等元素生物地球化学循环热点研究区域。目前微生物驱动的铁碳耦合是国际研究热点，而泥炭地发育过程中铁及其结合碳如何变化，微生物驱动机制都是亟待解决的科学问题。因此本项目从沉积历史过程、水文地貌类型及区域水热格局等不同尺度，阐明不同发育阶段泥炭地铁赋存状态、铁氧化物类型及结合碳含量，利用14C定年及2G模型探究泥炭形成发育过程中铁对有机碳累积效应；通过富集培养及高通量测序手段，开展泥炭地铁微生物功能类群的时空分布特征及演变规律研究；揭示铁还原菌对有机碳矿化及铁氧化菌对铁碳结合的作用机制，利用结构方程模型探究泥炭地发育-铁形态-微生物-碳累积之间耦合机制及互馈过程，揭示泥炭发育过程中铁对有机碳累积的微生物驱动机制。本成果将进一步丰富泥炭地形成发育及全球变化研究的基础理论知识，促进泥炭地学及湿地学的发展。	"Peatlands store one-third of global soil carbon, which is sensitive to climate change. The fluctuation of the peatlands make it be the hotspot of the iron, carbon and nitrogen biogeochemistry. Soil microbial communities couple iron and carbon biogeochemistry has been focused internationally, but the microbial regulation in the iron and iron bound organic should be focused during development of peatlands. So we will study the characteristics of the iron , iron oxidize and iron bound organic matter on different development stage through different temporal and spatial scales(depositional process, hydrogeography, regional hydrothermal pattern, etc.), and demonstrate iron bounding organic carbon accumulation by 14C ages of bulk soil organic matter and 2G model; Based on the method of  enrichment cultivation and high-throughput sequencing, we will explore the distribution of iron-oxidizing /reducing bacteria and its succession characteristics. We will also explain the mechanisms that how iron-reducing bacteria affects soil organic carbon mineralization and how iron-oxidizing bacteria affects the organic carbon acumullation.  Finally, the coupling mechanism and the connections among the development of peatlands, the iron variables, the microorganism and the organic carbon accumulation are studied by structural equation modeling, revealing that how microorganism affects iron and organic carbon accumulation during the development. The research, not only will enrich the basic theories of the development of peatlands and global change, but also will promote the development of the studies of peatlands and wetlands."	
城市土壤气态亚硝酸(HONO)排放与硝化微生物之间的关联机制	41771285	土壤生物学 ( D070104 )	杨小茹	副研究员	中国科学院城市环境研究所	63.00万元	面上项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2021 年 12 月 31 日	气态亚硝酸排放；硝化微生物；土壤微生物群落结构；土壤微生物活性；稳定同位素技术	nitrous acid (HONO) emission;nitrifying microbes;microbial community in soils; microbial activity in soils;stable isotope tracing technique	"气态亚硝酸(Nitrous Acid, HONO)，是城市环境的一种典型污染物。已有研究表明HONO排放存在一个很大的未知来源，其中一个重要来源是土壤硝化微生物作用下的直接排放。目前关于HONO排放的主要微生物过程研究仍鲜有报道。因此，在本研究中我们将选择不同城市化梯度的典型城市土壤――城市公园的草地、林地和城郊菜地作为主要研究对象，将原位测定和室内培养实验相结合，采用密闭箱收集法测定HONO浓度，获得不同土地利用方式下的城市土壤HONO排放规律；并应用微生物生态学技术，在DNA/RNA水平上比较土壤的总微生物和活性微生物群落结构及HONO排放相关的主要硝化微生物类群；进一步采用稳定同位素标记和添加抑制剂的方法，解析HONO排放的主要微生物过程以及好氧氨氧化细菌/古菌对HONO排放的相对贡献，以期阐明HONO排放和主要硝化微生物的关联机制，为HONO排放评估及调控提供更准确理论依据。"	"Nitrous acid (HONO) is a typical pollutant in urban environments. Field observations suggests a large proportion of unknown source of HONO, which was proposed to be attributed to the release of HONO from soil via microbial activity. Nitrifiers in soil play a major role in the formation of nitrite, which is the substrate for HONO emission. However, knowledge about the linkage between key nitrifiers and HONO emission is limited. In this proposal, we will collect soil samples with a gradient of urbanization in Xiamen, including the lawns and forest from parks in the urban area, and vegetable fields from the suburban area. By using high throughput sequencing and isotopic tracing, this project aims: 1) to characterize HONO emission in soils with different land uses by using flux chamber experiments on soil samples; 2) to depict the nitrification process linking to HONO production in both DNA and RNA levels; 3) to discriminate the key microbial process and the contribution of ammonia-oxidizing bacteria (AOB) and ammonia-oxidizing archaea (AOA) to the HONO emission by a combination of stable isotope tracing technique and inhibitor addition. Taken together, the results would reveal the key microbial process and identify key nitrifying players involved in HONO emission. And the finding in this study will also give us a comprehensive understanding of the ecology of AOB and AOA in urban soils and to provide insights into the effect of the land use on HONO emission in urban soils."	
稻田土壤生态系统好氧-厌氧氨氧化作用及其微生物介导机制	41771286	土壤生物学 ( D070104 )	钟文辉	教授	南京师范大学	63.00万元	面上项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2021 年 12 月 31 日	土壤氮循环；硝化细菌；土壤微生物；稻田土壤生态系统；分子生物学	Soil nitrogen cycle;Nitrifying microorganism;Soil microorganism;Paddy soil ecosystem;Molecular biology	微生物介导的氨氧化过程是土壤氮循环的中心和限速环节，主要分为好氧氨氧化、厌氧氨氧化和厌氧Fe(III)还原氨氧化三类过程。目前相关报道多数还局限在对各独立过程的研究，但自然生态系统中好氧-厌氧环境往往共存，上述三类具有相同底物或产物的氨氧化作用在“同一体系”下的空间分布规律及微生物介导机制尚不清楚。本项目拟以好氧-厌氧环境共存的稻田土壤为对象，利用微电极技术“同步原位测定”稻田水-土界面、根际及非根际土壤中DO、无机氮、pH等指标实时连续变化，研究三类氨氧化作用在稻田土壤生态系统中的空间分布规律，采用基因组技术、转录组技术等分子生态学手段分析各区域功能微生物分布及其介导机制，并模拟验证形成上述空间分布格局及微生物介导机制的关键环境因子及驱动机制。通过上述研究，本项目构建“同一体系”来阐明稻田土壤生态系统中好氧-厌氧氨氧化作用及其微生物介导机制，其结果将是土壤氮循环研究的一次创新与突破。	"The ammonia oxidation process mediated by microorganisms is a central and rate-limiting step in soil nitrogen cycle. It is comprised of three pathways including aerobic and anaerobic ammonia oxidation along with anaerobic ammonium oxidation coupled to Fe(III) reduction. Many recent studies focused on some single pathway. However, the aerobic and anaerobic conditions often co-exist in the natural ecosystem. As a result, it is still unclear of the spatial distribution and the mechanisms mediated by micro-organisms of the ammonia oxidation process with the same substrates or products, under the same system. In the present program, the paddy soil in which the aerobic and anaerobic conditions co-exist is used as the research subject. We attempted to 1) use the micro-electrode technique to study simultaneously and in situ the real time and continuous variation of DO, Eh and inorganic nitrogen, along with the spatial distribution of the three ammonia oxidation pathways in paddy field ecosystem; 2) study the spatial distribution of the functional microorganisms in different areas and the mechanisms mediated by micro-organisms; 3) simulate and validate the key environmental driving factors and related mechanisms that form the spatial distribution and the mechanisms mediated by micro-organisms. By achieving the studies above, this program aimed to construct the real “one system” to illustrate the aerobic and anaerobic ammonia oxidation and the mechanisms mediated by microorganisms. The results would be an innovation and breakthrough in the study of soil nitrogen cycle."	
喀斯特地区污染稻田自养型厌氧砷氧化的微生物机制	41771301	土壤生物学 ( D070104 )	孙蔚_	研究员	广东省生态环境技术研究所	63.00万元	面上项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2021 年 12 月 31 日	砷污染稻田土壤；喀斯特；自养型厌氧砷氧化；稳定同位素示踪；宏基因组	Arsenic contaminated rice paddy soil;Karst;Anaerobic oxidation of arsenite by autotrophic bacteria;Stable isotope probing;Metagenomics	西南喀斯特地区是我国重要稻米产区之一，但是该区域稻田土壤砷污染严重，影响人体健康，亟需相关方法解决砷污染问题。本项目针对喀斯特地区碳酸盐含量高这一特点，提出了自养型厌氧砷氧化的研究主题，聚焦于无机碳循环、砷循环与氮循环的耦联关系。主要通过以下三个方面展开工作：（1）通过地球化学手段来获取稻田土壤剖面中砷的赋存形式，从而探索自养型砷氧化在喀斯特地区稻田土壤中的地球化学印迹。（2）通过分子生物学手段分析稻田土壤中的微生物群落种群信息及其基因组学信息，探索微生物与环境污染因子的反馈及响应机制。（3）同时，使用稳定同位素示踪-宏基因组-单菌草图组装联用平台，揭示自养型砷氧化的功能微生物种属以及自养型砷氧化的代谢途径。本课题潜在的成果将对认识微生物驱动的砷循环，以及多元素（碳、氮、砷）耦联循环等基础科学问题有着重要意义，同时也能运用此理论知识指导污染修复实践。	"The Karst region is the major rice producing area in China. However, the rice paddy soil in this region are heavily contaminated by arsenic, which migrates the rice and threatens the human health. Attenuation of arsenic contamination in rice paddy soil is highly desired in this region. For this purpose, we propose the studies regarding the anaerobic arsenite oxidation by autotrophic bacteria in paddy soil. The proposed studies target on the elevated carbonate concentrations in Karst region and will explore the interactions between inorganic C, N, and As cycling. We aim (1) to investigate the concentrations of various arsenic species in different depth-resolved profiles of rice paddy soil to elucidate the geochemical evidence of anaerobic arsenite oxidation; (2) to characterize the innate microbiota to explore the microbial response to environmental factors such as various As species; (3) to illustrate the phylogenies of arsenite oxidizing bacteria and clarify the metabolic activities of arsenite oxidizing bacteria by coupling SIP,Metagenomics,and Contig binning. The results of the current study is critical to understand the microbially-mediated arsenic cycling and interplay between multiple elements cycling (C, N, and As). Such knowledge can be used to guide the engineering practice to remediate As contamination in rice paddies as well."	
成土早期微生物碳需求对土壤有机磷矿化的驱动作用	41701288	土壤生物学 ( D070104 )	王吉鹏	讲师	成都理工大学	25.00万元	青年科学基金项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2020 年 12 月 31 日	土壤磷转化过程；矿化作用；土壤酶；生态化学计量；同位素技术	soil phosphorus transformation process;mineralization;soil enzyme;ecological stoichiometry;isotope technique	微生物参与的土壤有机磷（P）矿化是成土早期生物有效态P的重要来源。阐明微生物碳（C）需求对土壤有机P矿化的驱动作用是理解成土早期土壤有机P矿化机理的关键。本项目拟选取贡嘎山海螺沟冰川退缩区土壤年代序列（约120年），开展野外土壤调查和室内土壤培养实验，研究微生物C需求对土壤有机P矿化的驱动作用。通过土壤酶活性分析，评估微生物C需求对土壤有机P潜在矿化速率的影响；通过土壤微生物化学计量比调查、养分添加实验和土壤磷酸根氧同位素测定，评估微生物C需求对土壤有机P矿化产物归趋的影响；最终阐明成土早期微生物C需求对土壤有机P矿化的驱动作用。研究结果有助于加深对成土早期土壤有机P矿化机理的理解，也为认识成土早期土壤P转化和植被演替的联系，实现裸地植被快速和稳定的恢复提供理论支持。	"During the early stage of soil development, mineralization of soil organic phosphorus (P; organic P, Po) mediated by microbes is a major source of bioavailable P, and it is necessary to decipher the driving effects of microbial carbon (C) demand for a better understanding of Po mineralization. In this proposed project, the 120-year-old Hailuogou chronosequence in Gongga Mountain is selected, and field soil surveys and laboratory soil incubation experiments will be conducted to investigate the driving effects of microbial C demand on soil Po mineralization. Soil enzyme analysis will be used to study the influence of microbial C demand on potential Po mineralization rate; microbial stoichiometry survey, nutrient addition experiment and oxygen isotope analysis of soil phosphate will be used to study the influence of microbial C demand on the fate of Po mineralization products; based on these data, the driving effects of microbial C demand on Po mineralization during the early stage of soil development will be illuminated. The proposed project will contribute to a better understanding of soil Po mineralization during the early stage of soil development, and will also help to link soil P transformation to plant succession and provide a theoretical basis for the efficient and stable vegetation restoration of bare lands."	
农田黑土旱田改稻田土壤氮素转化与关键微生物特性研究	41701289	土壤生物学 ( D070104 )	李鑫	讲师	东北农业大学	24.00万元	青年科学基金项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2020 年 12 月 31 日	土壤氮循环；土壤微生物多样性；氨氧化细菌；反硝化细菌；微生物基因组	soil nitrogen cycle;soil microbial diversity;ammonia-oxidizing bacteria;denitrifying bacteria;microbial genome	农产品的结构性调整和经济效益驱动，黑龙江省水稻面积达到5300万亩，大面积旱田改种为稻田，易使土壤养分及微生物受到影响。为保护我国黑土资源，有必要从氮素转化及关键土壤微生物方面探究黑土旱田改稻田后的变化特征，本项目利用黑土旱田改稻田后的系列耕层土壤为研究对象，拟采用q-PCR、MiSeq测序和微生物基因芯片微阵列技术，结合黑土的理化性质，重点研究：（1）农田黑土氮素转化及相关土壤微生物（氨氧化细菌、古菌和反硝化细菌等）对旱田改稻田的响应规律及主控因素；（2）探讨旱田改稻田对农田黑土氮转化过程中关键功能基因丰度以及相关微生物群落变化的影响；（3）从微生物功能基因多样性层面分析土壤功能微生物类群，阐明旱田改稻田后参与氮素循环并占主导地位的微生物菌群差异。项目产出成果有助于人们更全面地理解旱田改稻田的土壤氮素循环及微生物调控机制，旱田改稻田土壤肥力的变化趋势，为保护和利用黑土资源提供理论支撑。	"The drive of structural adjustment and economic benefits of agricultural products, the area of rice has reached 5.3 million hectares in Heilongjiang province. Make paddy soil nutrients and microorganisms easily affected when a large area of upland had been changed to paddy. In order to protect mollisoil resources in our country, it is necessary to explore the characteristic of this change on nitrogen transformation and key microorganism in mollisoil after upland had been changed to paddy. In this project, we use the mollisoil after which land use had been changed as the research object, using q-PCR, MiSeq high-throughput sequencing and microarray technology, and the combination of conventional physicochemical method, focusing on (1): Responses of nitrogen transformations and key microorganism (ammonia oxidizing bacteria, ammonia oxidizing Achaea and denitrifying bacteria) to land use change from upland to paddy field in mollisoil farmland, and main controlling factors; (2) investigating the effect of change from upland to paddy on key functional genes abundance and related microbial communities in the process of soil nitrogen transformation; (3) analyzing of microbial groups in the soil from the aspect of microbial functional gene diversity. Clarify dominant microbial flora which involved in soil nitrogen nutrient cycling in the cropping system and bacterial community difference. The project output will help people more comprehensive understanding of drought change paddy soil nitrogen cycling and microbial control mechanism, the change trend of drought to paddy soil fertility, and provide theoretical support for the conservation and utilization of soil resources."	
青藏高原典型高寒草甸土壤微生物对增温和降水改变的响应	41701298	土壤生物学 ( D070104 )	时玉	助理研究员	中国科学院南京土壤研究所	26.00万元	青年科学基金项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2020 年 12 月 31 日	土壤微生物群落结构；土壤微生物多样性；土壤微生物生物地理；生物信息学；气候变化	Soil microbial community structure;Soil microbial diversity;Soil microbial biogeography;Bioinfomatics;Climate change	青藏高原高寒草甸作为我国主要的草地畜牧区，气温升高幅度高于全球平均水平，对环境变化和人为扰动具有更加显著的响应。土壤微生物在土壤的养分循环过程中占有非常重要的作用，微生物的群落组成与草场的质量以及草场退化后的修复息息相关。然而，在该地区，长期的增温或降雨改变以及增温降雨交互作用会对地下生态系统尤其是地下土壤微生物群落带来怎样的影响，其变化规律如何，还需进一步研究。本申请项目拟利用在青藏高原典型高寒草甸土壤建立的野外模拟增温和降雨交互实验平台，利用高通量测序技术，研究增温和降雨对土壤微生物群落组成与多样性的影响；分析增温降雨交互作用下土壤微生物群落的响应；在时间梯度下分析土壤微生物多样性及群落组成的变化规律，找到敏感土壤微生物菌群指标，预测其变化趋势；以期揭示土壤微生物对外界气候环境变化的响应及反馈机制。	"Alpine grassland of the Tibetan Plateau is the main livestock area. This area is more sensitive to environmental changes and human disturbance, and the rate of increase in surface air temperatures is faster than the average global rate. Soil microbial community are important in soil nutrition cycling, and also strong correlated with the quality of the pasture and the repair after grassland degradation. However, the influence such as warming, precipitation and warming integrated with altered precipitation under time gradient on the belowground system especially the soil microbial communities, and their varying trend were poorly understood. Based on simulate precipitation and warming experiment in Tibetan Plateau alpine meadow, using the High throughput sequencing, we want to investigate the effect of warming and altered precipitation on the soil microbial community, and the response of soil microbial community to warming integrated with altered precipitation, analysis the variation of soil microbial diversity and community under the temporal gradient, find some phyla which are sensitive to climate changes and predict variation tendency of these phyla. In a word, this study will illustrate the response and feedback mechanism of soil microbial community to climate change."	
北京东灵山林线上下土壤微生物的时空分异研究	41701273	土壤生物学 ( D070104 )	申聪聪	助理研究员	中国科学院生态环境研究中心	26.00万元	青年科学基金项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2020 年 12 月 31 日	土壤微生物生物地理；微生物多样性与功能；山地生态系统；林线	soil microbial biogeography;microbial diversity and function;montane ecosystem;treeline	山地生态系统是研究土壤微生物时空分异规律的理想环境。高山林线作为垂直自然带上的一条重要的生态系统分界线，对气候变化极为敏感。气候变暖可能导致林线向海拔更高处迁移，然而林线附近土壤微生物群落和功能如何变化却很少有人关注。近些年研究者在揭示土壤微生物海拔分布规律方面取得了很大进展，但对于微生物时间动态的变化规律、微生物时空分布的潜在影响机制及微生物群落与功能的关系，这些方面的认知仍然十分有限。本项目拟选择北京东灵山为研究对象，针对林线上下不同植被类型土壤，采集不同时间梯度和海拔梯度土壤样品，研究土壤特性、微生物群落和功能的时间动态变化和海拔分布规律。通过这些研究，系统了解山地生态系统不同植被类型土壤微生物群落和功能的时间动态变化规律，阐明林线上下土壤微生物群落和功能的分异规律及驱动机制，揭示土壤微生物群落与功能的关系，进而为预测山地生态系统对气候变化的响应提供理论依据。	"Montane ecosystem is an ideal environment for studying temporal and spatial variations in soil microbial communities. Alpine treeline, as an important ecosystem boundary of natural vertical zones, is extremely sensitive to climate change. Climate warming leads to movement of the treeline toward a higher elevation, but little is known about the dynamics of microbial communities and functions under this change. Though encouraging progress has been made on elevational distribution of microbial communities recently, our knowledge of microbial temporal variations and underlying mechanisms of community assembly is still limited, as well as the relationship between microbial communities and functions. This project intends to select soil samples of two different vegetation types above and below treeline on Dongling Mountain, Beijing. Soil samples will be collected in different temporal gradient and elevational gradient, aiming to study temporal and elevational variations for soil characteristics, microbial communities and soil multifunctionality. Our project will be benefit for understanding dynamics of soil microbial communities and functions, underlying mechanisms of temporal and elevational microbial diversity patterns, and relationships between microbial communities and functions. These results can also provide theoretical basis for predicting the responses of montane ecosystems to climate change."	
微生物辅助N掺杂石墨烯量子点/MOFs复合材料光电催化还原CO2	51703151	有机无机复合功能材料 ( E030905 )	杨慧敏	讲师	太原理工大学	23.00万元	青年科学基金项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2020 年 12 月 31 日	CO2还原；N掺杂石墨烯量子点；金属有机骨架材料；光电催化；微生物阳极	CO2 reduction;N-doped graphene quantum dots;Metal-organic frameworks;photoelectrocatalysis;microbial anode	将CO2转化为低碳能源，具有解决能源和环境问题的双重意义。本项目提出一种微生物辅助光电催化还原CO2的新体系，将N掺杂石墨烯量子点和MOFs进行复合作为光电催化阴极，含有离子液体的多元溶剂体系为阴极电解液，利用在线训化法获得具有电活性的微生物阳极，构建光电催化还原CO2为低碳能源的新体系。考察N掺杂石墨烯量子点和MOFs的复合方式和结构对催化CO2还原的作用机制，探索多元电解液各组分对提高CO2溶解度、降低过电位和抑制竞争析氢反应的影响规律以及考察微生物阳极为阴极提供电子和质子的能力，重点研究该复合催化剂对C=O键的活化机制，同时通过第一性原理计算N掺杂石墨烯量子点/MOFs的能带结构、构效关系及CO2在催化剂表面的吸附位点、中间过渡态和反应活化能等，设计反应历程，寻找低能量反应路径。将理论计算与实验相结合，探讨微生物辅助N掺杂石墨烯量子点/MOFs光电催化还原CO2过程中的基本科学问题。	"It has a double meaning to solve energy shortages and environmental problems if dioxide carbon can be converted to low-carbon energy. This project proposes a new system of photocatalytic reduction of CO2 assisted by microorganism. The photoelectrocatalysis system of CO2 reduction is designed and assembled by using photo-electro-catalyst of N-doped graphene quantum dots/MOFs composite as cathode, the multi-solvent system containing ionic liquid is chosen as catholyte and the electroactive microbial anode is prepared by on-line domesticated method. The mechanism of the composite mode and structure between N-doped graphene quantum dots and MOFs on the catalytic reduction of CO2 are investigated. The effect laws of components of multi-solvent catholyte on improving CO2 solubility, reducing overpotential and inhibiting competitive hydrogen evolution are explored. The ability of different microbial anodes to provide electrons and protons for cathodes is also investigated. The project mainly discusses the cation mechanism of catalysts on C=O activation. Meanwhile, first principle calculation method is used to calculate the band structure and structure-activity relationship of the N-doped graphene quantum dots/MOFs, and the adsorption site, intermediate transition state and reaction activation energy of CO2 on the catalyst surface. Designing the reaction process to find a low energy response path. Combining theory calculation and experiment, this project discusses the basic scientific problems in the process of microorganism assisted N-doped graphene quantum dots/MOFs composites photocatalytic reduction of CO2."	
压力延迟渗透耦合微生物燃料电池处理排海污水同步产能研究	51708408	污水处理与资源化 ( E080402 )	薛文超	副研究员	天津工业大学	24.00万元	青年科学基金项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2020 年 12 月 31 日	压力延迟渗透；微生物燃料电池；耦合技术；污水处理；协同产能	Pressure retarded osmosis;Microbial fuel cell;Coupled technology;Wastewater treatment;Simultaneous energy generation	正渗透技术及微生物电化学系统等新型低能耗污水处理技术的发展为有效处理排海污水并回收污水中的资源和能源提供了基础。本项目提出将压力延迟渗透技术与微生物燃料电池技术相结合，采用渗透膜替代离子交换膜，同时完成污水微生物处理及膜分离排放，生物产电及盐差发电等功能，并通过调节耦合系统操作压力实现微生物处理与渗透传质过程的速率匹配，以期实现最大限度的回收和利用排海污水中的能源。.首先，对压力延迟渗透膜进行高效抗污染改良，建立高通量抗污染的渗透微生物燃料电池系统。在此基础上，构建压力延迟渗透-微生物燃料电池耦合工艺，并对系统的传质-产能机制通过理论模型进行解析。通过对工艺性能的优化和工艺原理的阐明，本项目将为以低能耗实现污水安全排海及能源回收提供新的思路和理论依据。	"Efficient treatment of wastewater with low energy cost is a promising solution for controlling the severe costal pollution problems in China. Various innovative technologies such as seawater driven osmotic membrane processes and bioelectrochemical systems have been robustly developed, providing alternatives to achieve energy-efficient wastewater treatment and discharge. In this study, we propose a synergy of pressure retarded osmosis and microbial fuel cell technologies, namely a pressure retarded microbial osmotic fuel cell, with the function of simultaneously wastewater purification and transmembrane discharge with electricity generation by using an osmotic membrane to substitute an ion exchange membrane. Furthermore, the mass transportation rate through the osmotic membrane will be matched with the rate of microbial treatment by adjusting the operational pressure in order to obtain an optimal performance in terms of wastewater purification and energy production in the system. .To establish a highly fouling resistant osmotic microbial fuel cell system, membrane surface modification will be initially performed in order to improve the anti-fouling performance of a pressure retarded osmotic membrane. Afterward, a pressure retarded microbial osmotic fuel cell process will be developed, followed by interpretation of mass transport and energy generation mechanisms in the combined system using modeling method. By optimizing process performance and understanding the mechanisms, this study will provide an innovative concept and theoretical support for safe disposal of treated wastewater as well as energy recovery from wastewater."	
抗生素对堆肥中关键功能微生物驱动硝化作用的影响机制研究	51708093	城镇固体废弃物处置与资源化 ( E080404 )	张旭	助理研究员	东北农业大学	25.00万元	青年科学基金项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2020 年 12 月 31 日	硝化速率；功能基因；抗生素；氨氧化细菌；氨氧化古菌	nitrification rate;functional gene;antibiotics;ammonia-oxidizing bacteria;ammonia-oxidizing archaea	高温好氧堆肥是无害化处理和资源化利用畜禽粪便的重要途径之一。针对畜禽粪便中残留的抗生素对堆肥硝化作用的影响机制研究不足等问题。本研究利用实时定量PCR和16S rDNA高通量测序技术手段，拟阐明抗生素的含量和抗生素抗性基因对堆肥中硝化速率的响应规律，以及抗生素对功能微生物氨氧化细菌和氨氧化古群落结构和关键因子amoA基因丰度的影响。结合结构方程模型，揭示堆肥过程中硝化速率与抗生素含量和抗性基因丰度、微生境因子、关键功能微生物群落结构和amoA基因丰度的交互作用机制。利用基因共表达网络调控分析的预测方法，建立堆肥过程中抗生素抗性基因-微生境关键影响因子-关键功能微生物活性-硝化速率调控技术体系。为减少堆肥中氮素损失，促进含畜禽粪便的无害化处理及资源化利用提供技术支撑。	"High temperature aerobic composting is an effective approach for stabilizing livestock waste via the biological degradation of organic matter, which has been shown to be effective in reducing the levels of persistent organic pollutants such as veterinary antibiotics. This study aims to illuminate the mechanism and effect of residual antibiotics in livestock manure on the nitrification during composting. Real-time PCR and 16S rDNA High-Throughput Sequencing techniques will be employed to characterize the effect of antibiotic contents and antibiotic resistance genes (ARGs) on nitrification rate, and aims to light the influences of antibiotics on the structure of ammonia oxidizing bacteria and ammonia-oxidizing archaea communities, and the abundance of amoA gene. Then the structural equation model (SEMs) is adopted to reveal the interaction among the nitrification rate in composting, the concentration of antibiotic, the abundance of resistance gene, the microhabitat factors, the community structure of key functional microbial, and the abundance of amoA gene. Based on Gene Co-expression Network Analysis prediction method, ARGs, the key factors microhabitat, the activity of key functional microorganism, and the nitrification rate regulating technical system will be established. This study can provide a technical support for reducing nitrogen loss in compost and promoting innocuity and resource livestock manure compost."	
废水生物处理过程中微生物代谢产物的作用机制与调控原理	51738012	工程结构 ( E0804 )	盛国平	教授	中国科学技术大学	300.00万元	重点项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2022 年 12 月 31 日	微生物代谢产物；污水生物处理；深度处理；调控；相互作用	Microbial metabolic products;Biological wastewater treatment;Advanced treatment;Manipulation;Interaction	生物处理工艺是我国城市污水处理的主要手段，反应器中微生物在降解污染物的同时分泌大量的代谢产物（如EPS、SMP等），它们含有丰富的官能团，可以和污染物发生复杂的相互作用，影响污染物的存在形态和降解过程，但由于其成分结构复杂多变，研究者对其在污染物高效转化过程中的微观作用认识不足。因此系统研究废水生物处理过程中微生物代谢产物的形成机制，深入认识其在废水处理过程中的重要作用，是水污染控制领域的一个重要研究方向。本申请项目拟通过解析微生物代谢产物的形成特性，表征其与重金属、微污染物和营养元素的相互作用，阐明微生物产物在生物处理和深度处理过程中的作用机制，实现微生物产物产生的调控，提高废水生物处理及后续深度处理的效率，实现污染物的高效去除。该项目研究对于了解废水生物处理过程的内在微观机制、优化废水生物处理工艺、提高污染物去除效率，有着重要的理论意义和实际价值。	"Biological process is the main technique for wastewater treatment in China. Microorganisms in the biological treatment reactors will secreted plenty of biomolecules, such as extracellular polymeric substances (EPS), soluble microbial products (SMP), which play important roles in the biological wastewater treatment process. These microbial metabolic products contains plenty of functional groups and huge surface areas to interact with various pollutants, and thus influence the fate of pollutants in bioreactors. However, due to the complex compositions of EPS, their crucial roles in the pollutants conversion and degradation. Thus, it is an important issue to explore the formation and roles of the microbial metabolic products in biological wastewater treatment process. In this propose, sensitive analysis methods will be proposed to characterize the interaction between microbial metabolic products and various pollutants (e.g., heavy metals, micropollutants, nutrients etc). The roles of the microbial metabolic products in the enhanced removal of pollutants in biological treatment and advanced treatment processes will be clarified. The optimized strategies to manipulate the production and characteristics of microbial metabolic products will be proposed to improve the removal of various pollutants in biological wastewater treatment and advanced treatment processes. The results will provide a scientific basis to improve removal efficiency of pollutants in biological wastewater treatment."	
低浓度抗生素胁迫下城市给水管网管壁生物膜特性及微生物多样性研究	51778453	城镇给排水系统 ( E080403 )	张永吉	副教授	同济大学	62.00万元	面上项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2021 年 12 月 31 日	给水管网；生物膜；抗生素；微生物多样性；胁迫	drinking water distribution system;biofilm;antibiotic;microbial diversity ;stress	城市给水管网的管壁生物膜会对造成水中微生物超标，而城市给水管网水中检出的抗性细菌和抗性基因对人类健康造成了潜在威胁。本项目通过分子生物学手段，对给水管壁生物膜中抗性细菌进行鉴定，揭示抗生素对给水管壁生物膜中抗性细菌形成的影响，研究抗生素胁迫下给水管壁生物膜中菌种群多样性和群落演替规律，解析抗生素在管壁生物膜形成中的作用。通过对抗生素作用下管壁生物膜中抗性基因的转移的基因学研究，揭示给水管壁生物膜中抗性菌和抗性基因的形成和转移过程，并建立抗性基因存在下的给水管网水生物安全性评价方法，探索基于低浓度抗生素胁迫下城市给水管网管壁生物膜调控方法和抗性菌种群的调控机制，为给水管壁生物膜的控制和提高给水管网水质提供科学依据和技术支持。	"Urban water supply network is an important part of the water supply system. The microbes in the water supply network can attach to the tube wall to form the biomembrane which will fall off the water with aging and cause the microorganisms in the water pipe to exceed the standard. In recent years, Resistant bacteria and resistance genes detected in water in urban water supply networks in recent years have posed a potential threat to human health. By means of molecular biology, this project will identify the resistant bacteria in the biomembrane on the water supply pipe wall, reveal the effect of antibiotics on the formation of resistant bacteria in biomembrane of water supply pipe wall, study the diversity and community succession of bacteria in the biofilm of water pipe wall under the action of antibiotics, and analyse the role of antibiotics in the formation of biofilm in the wall. Based on the genetic study of the resistance gene transfer in the biofilm of the wall under the action of antibiotics, the formation process of the resistant bacteria and resistance genes in the biofilm of the water supply wall will be revealed, and water biological safety assessment method for water supply network in the presence of resistance gene will be established. Also, the project will explore the regulation mechanism of the biofilm of the urban water supply network under the low concentration of antibiotic stress and the regulation mechanism of the resistant bacteria population. It can provide scientific basis and technical support for the control of biofilm of water supply wall, and the basis for improving the water quality of drinking water in water supply network."	
嗜酸微生物作用下黄铜矿多步氧化分解的协同作用机制	51774332	湿法冶金 ( E041202 )	王军	教授	中南大学	60.00万元	面上项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2021 年 12 月 31 日	生物浸出；黄铜矿；浸矿微生物；浸出动力学；生物浸出机理	bioleaching;chalcopyrite;bioleaching bacteria;leaching kinetics;bioleaching mechanism	黄铜矿是自然界最重要的铜矿资源，其生物冶金是研究的热点和难点。针对不同产地不同晶型的黄铜矿，筛选培育并构建专属高效的浸矿微生物种群组合，综合运用高性能计算，宏基因组学、AMICSCAN、XAFS、电化学-同步辐射XRD等多种先进的研究手段，阐明黄铜矿生物浸出体系的微生物种群演替规律以及主要离子组分、溶解氧、中间产物等关键组分对浸出过程的影响规律；研究黄铜矿微生物浸出过程的复杂化学反应，实时原位研究矿物溶解过程精细的物相变化和化学元素转化规律；深入系统解析黄铜矿生物冶金体系多元组分行为与界面作用机制，阐明不同微生物作用下黄铜矿的氧化、钝化与溶解过程的影响因素；揭示黄铜矿生物冶金体系关键组分协同作用机制及其反应机理，进一步实现黄铜矿生物强化浸出，为改善黄铜矿生物浸出过程动力学提供理论依据。研究将进一步加深对黄铜矿微生物浸出机理的认识，对推进黄铜矿生物冶金产业化具有重要的理论指导意义。	"Chalcopyrite is one of the most plentiful and widespread copper-bearing minerals in nature, and recently bioleaching has become a hotspot and difficultly in the flied of the copper extraction technology. The chalcopyrite of different producing area and different crystal type are chosen in this work, the exclusive efficient combination of the acidophilic microorganism communication is screened and cultured in the first step, and then the communication succession and the influence rule of key components containing main ion composition, dissolved oxygen, intermediate products etc. are clarified by the integrated use of high performance computing, macro genomics, electrochemical synchrotron radiation, AMICSCAN, XAFS, XRD and other advanced research methods during the bioleaching process. The complexed chemical reaction during the bioleaching process of chalcopyrite was studied. And the law of delicately phase transformation and the change rule of the chemical elements was explored by the in-stiu techniques to further deepen the systematically comprehension of the interaction mechanisms between the multiple component behaviours and interfacial changes. At last, through the above ways, this work can be clarified the influence factors of chalcopyrite oxidation, passivation and dissolution process with different acidophilic microorganism and revealed the synergistic effect and reaction mechanism of key solution constituent in the chalcopyrite bioleaching system. Finally, it could be providing the theoretical basis for improving the dissolution kinetics and the ways of strengthening the bioleaching process of chalcopyrite. The research results can help to deepen our further understanding the mechanisms of chalcopyrite bioleaching, and it also is of great theoretical significance and application value to the industrialization of low grade copper sulphide ores biohydrometallurgy."	
水工混凝土构筑物微生物群落特性及其对混凝土性能的影响机制	51779076	水环境污染与修复 ( E090301 )	李轶	教授	河海大学	61.00万元	面上项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2021 年 12 月 31 日	水工构筑物 ；水动力；微生物群落；功能菌；混凝土性能	Water conservancy and hydropower engineering;Hydrodynamics;Microbial community;Functional microorganisms;Concrete property	水工混凝土是水利工程主要的建筑材料，其在不同环境条件下的稳定性能是水利工程安全运行的重要保障。处在潮湿环境中的水工混凝土表面和孔隙中生长大量微生物，会通过不同的途径对混凝土产生腐蚀或修复等作用，从而影响混凝土性能。目前对水利工程中水工混凝土微生物作用的认识仍不清楚。项目拟通过野外观测和室内模拟等手段，采用高通量测序等方法，以长江流域典型水工构筑物所在水体为研究区域，以水工混凝土微生物群落为研究对象，研究水工混凝土微生物群落的时空分布规律，解析水动力条件下水工混凝土微生物群落响应机制，建立水动力条件下微生物群落与主导环境因子的数值关系；再研究水工混凝土微生物群落与混凝土性能变化的关联性，明确对混凝土具有腐蚀和修复作用的功能微生物，阐明水动力条件下水工混凝土关键功能微生物对混凝土的作用机制，建立耦合微生物作用的水工混凝土构筑物强度预测模型，为保障水工混凝土构筑物的安全运行提供理论指导。	"Hydraulic concrete is one of the most fundamental construction materials in water conservancy projects (WCPs). The structural stability of hydraulic concrete is an important guarantee for the safe operations of WCPs. A large number of microorganisms live on the surface and within the pores of hydraulic concrete structures (HCSs) under humid conditions. These microorganisms can lead to either corrosion or repairation of concrete by different ways, thus affecting the properties of concretes. However, the knowledge on the effects of microorganisms on the properties of HCSs in WCPs is still lacking. By using high throughput sequencing analysis, metagenome analysis and other bioinformatics methods, the spatial and temporal distribution of microbial community on and within typical HCSs in the Yangtze River Basin will be firstly revealed in field research. Then indoor simulation experiments will be performed and the microbial community structures and function expressions under environmental factors, e.g., hydraulic disturbance, will be identified. Afterwards, the influencing mechanism of functional microorganisms on the properties of HCSs will be clarified and the relationship between functional microorganism succession and changes in the performance of HCSs will be revealed. Finally, a strength prediction model of HCSs coupled microbial action will be established to provide the theoretical support for the safe operations of WCPs."

眼表微生物组的改变参与过敏性结膜炎发病机制的研究	81700803	角膜及眼表疾病 ( H1201 )	文小凤	博士后	中山大学	20.00万元	青年科学基金项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2020 年 12 月 31 日	过敏性结膜炎；眼表微生物组；全基因组测序	allergic conjunctivitis;conjunctival microbiota;metagenomic shotgun sequencing 	人体的眼表定植着相对稳定的微生物群落，微生物组的改变与包括过敏性疾病在内的多种免疫介导疾病相关。我们前期的研究结果表明空气中PM2.5浓度的升高，可以通过调控眼表微生物组中痤疮丙酸杆菌和绿脓假单胞菌的相对丰度诱发炎症，从而导致眼表角结膜的损伤。由于眼表的健康与眼表微生物密切相关，因而我们提出过敏性结膜炎的病程可能与眼表微生物的改变有关这一假说。已有研究表明金黄色葡萄球菌可能与慢性过敏性结膜炎的病理生理机制有关，葡萄球菌肠毒素、剥脱性毒素等金黄色葡萄球菌的代谢产物也被证实与过敏性疾病相关。然而由于研究手段的局限性，目前的研究尚不能全面系统地对过敏性结膜炎患者眼表微生物组的改变进行揭示。因而本研究试图在前期研究结果的基础上，通过宏基因组测序手段，找到眼表微生物组中与过敏性结膜炎发病相关的微生物种类，最终达到以该微生物种群为靶点来调节眼表的免疫状态，为过敏性结膜炎新的治疗方式的探索提供依据。	"Microbial ecosystems interact with the human body and affect human health. Ocular microbiota plays a key role in maintaining the physiology of the ocular surface, and dysbiosis of local microbial community can lead to ocular surface diseases. Using direct metagenomic shotgun sequencing approach, we surveyed the composition and function of conjunctival microbiota in volunteers from three Chinese cities (Guangzhou, Wenzhou, and Beijing) and showed that the airborne particulate matter PM2.5 from Beijing modulated conjunctival microbiota and damaged ocular surface. So we hypothesize that the alteration of the ocular surface microbiome may be associated with allergic conjunctivitis. Allergic conjunctivitis is a common form of ocular allergy, as it affects nearly one-third of the world population. As an inflammation condition of the conjunctiva tissue, allergic conjunctivitis is triggered by IgE-mediated and/or non-IgE-mediated allergic responses to allergens interacting with toll-like receptor 2. The role of Staphylococcus aureus colonization in the pathophysiology of chronic allergic conjunctivitis has been suggested, and the products of S. aureus, such as staphylococcal enterotoxin (SE) and exfoliative toxin, are correlated with allergic diseases. However, due to the limitations of traditional culture-based research methods, whether and how the ocular surface microbiota changes in allergic conjunctivitis patients remain unknown. Therefore, we will survey the composition and function of the conjunctival microbiome on allergic conjunctivitis patients using the direct metagenomic shotgun sequencing approach."	
基于银屑病患者肠道微生物宏基因组学的银屑灵干预机制研究	81704081	中医外科 ( H2709 )	闫玉红	副主任医师	广州中医药大学	20.00万元	青年科学基金项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2020 年 12 月 31 日	银屑病；肠道微生物；宏基因组学；银屑灵方	Psoriasis;Intestinal microflora;Metagenomics;Chinese Herbs Yinxielin	皮肤和粘膜同为人体免疫的第一道防线，肠道微生物影响免疫细胞的产生，肠道菌群结构的改变与慢性代谢性疾病的发生发展密切相关。肠道疾病在银屑病的常见并发症中位居第二，已知Th-17同时与克罗恩病、溃疡性结肠炎、银屑病和关节炎相关。课题组前期抽样观察银屑病患者中部分患者存在大便性状改变，口服中药对患者大便有改善作用；且已发现中药复方葛根芩连汤的降糖效果可能与改变肠道菌群的作用相关。因此我们提出科学假说：肠道微生态和免疫微环境是银屑病发病的重要原因，中医药通过直接作用于肠道菌群达到治疗作用。高通量测序技术使肠道微生物宏基因组全面测序分析成为可能，本研究通过对银屑病人肠道微生物宏基因组的测定及标识，同时采用国医大师_国维教授治疗银屑病的经验方银屑灵对患者进行验证，观察宏基因组和生物标记物能否回落，从宏基因组学的角度探讨银屑病患者肠道微环境的变化，及其与银屑病发生、发展之间的关系及中医药可能的作用机制。	"Skin and mucous membrane with the first line of defense of the human body, intestinal microbial effects of immune cells, its structure changes and the development are closely related to chronic metabolic diseases. Intestinal disease is the second most common complication of psoriasis, and Th-17 is known to be associated with Crohn's disease, ulcerative colitis, psoriasis and arthritis. Our previous researches showed that the hypoglycemic effect of Gegenqianlian decoction could be related to the change of intestinal microflora. The effect of traditional Chinese medicine on the stool of patients with psoriasis was observed. Therefore, we put forward the scientific hypothesis: intestinal micro-ecological and immune microenvironment is an important reason for the incidence of psoriasis, Chinese medicine directly through the role of intestinal flora to achieve therapeutic effect. High-throughput sequencing technology makes the comprehensive sequencing analysis of intestinal microbial macro genome possible. Through the determination and identification of macrobente microorganism in psoriasis patients, the author has adopted the experience of Professor Guo Guowei, To investigate the changes of intestinal microenvironment in patients with psoriasis and its relationship with the occurrence and development of psoriasis, and to explore the relationship between macrobacteria and biomarkers, as well as its possible mechanism of action."	
面向食品安全微生物预测的异构关联模糊系统建模关键技术及实证	61772239	新应用领域中的基础研究 ( F020517 )	邓赵红	教授	江南大学	64.00万元	面上项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2021 年 12 月 31 日	食品安全微生物预测；异构关联；模糊系统；精简学习；深度模糊推理	Food Security Microbial Prediction;Heterogeneous Relevance;Fuzzy Systems;Concision Learning;Deep Fuzzy Inference	预测微生物学在食品安全领域具有重要的应用价值。微生物预测模型构建作为预测微生物学的核心技术，当前还面临诸如如何增强预测模型的不确定知识表示能力、不确定建模能力、可解释性以及异构关联场景的知识调控和协作等挑战。针对此，本课题拟探讨面向食品安全微生物预测的异构关联模糊智能模型建模关键技术及实证。主要研究内容包括：面向食品安全微生物预测的高解释性模糊不确定知识表达和预测模型结构；增强模糊不确定智能预测模型解释性的精简学习技术和算法；关联异构场景的食品微生物预测模型的异构域知识调控和多任务协作机制及学习算法；大规模异构数据驱动的食品安全深度模糊不确定微生物预测模型构建及可扩展学习技术；以及模糊不确定微生物预测模型在食品安全典型应用中的有效性评估机制和实证研究。课题组已有的模糊不确定智能模型构建和微生物过程智能建模方面的研究基础为本课题的有效实施提供了充分的准备。	"Predictive microbiology has important application value in the field of food safety. As the core technology of predictive microbiology, the microbial prediction model construction still faces many challenges, such as how to enhance the abilities of prediction model for uncertain knowledge representation, uncertain modeling, interpretability, knowledge regulation and collaboration of the heterogeneous relevant scenes. According to these challenges, this project is proposed to explore microbial food safety oriented key techniques of the heterogeneous relavent fuzzy intelligent prediction model and its empirical study. Main research contents include the following aspects: The high interpretable uncertain knowledge representation and model structure for microbial food safety microbial prediction; The learning techniques and algorithms for conciseness enhancement of fuzzy uncertain intelligent prediction model; The heterogeneous regulation and collaboration mechanism and the corresponding learning algorithms in the heterogeneous relevant scenario and multi-task scenario for fuzzy uncertain microbial prediction model; Large-scale heterogeneous data driven fuzzy uncertainty deep prediction model construction and the scalable learning techniques; The comprehensive effectiveness evaluation mechanism of food safty prediction model in the typical applications and the empirical study of the proposed fuzzy uncertainty microbial prediction techniques. The research outputs about fuzzy uncertain intelligent model techniques in our previous work and their applications in microbial process modeling have provided a solid foundation for the effective implementation of this project."
