用于水圈微生物代谢分析的单细胞基因表达技术的研发及其应用	91751102	微生物研究的其他新技术方法 ( C010403 )	张卫文	教授	天津大学	80.00万元	重大研究计划	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2020 年 12 月 31 日	单细胞分析；未培养微生物；转录组分析；海洋蓝细菌；代谢和调控机制	Single-cell analysis;Unculturable microbes;Transcriptomics;Ocean cyanobacteria;Metabolic and regulatory mechanisms	"水圈微生物的生理生态功能研究面临诸多的挑战，其中的两个是：一）超过99％的环境微生物无法在实验室中获得培养；二）对于能够实现培养的微生物，由于实验室培养条件很难完全重现其天然生存环境，因而造成从纯培养获得的知识不能充分体现自然界生存的微生物的生理功能。针对这些挑战，本申请将发展和应用微生物单细胞基因表达分析技术对海洋环境中的光合蓝细菌的生理生态学进行研究，解析在典型大洋生态环境中起关键功能的海洋蓝细菌的代谢新途径及新调控机制。具体目标：一）优化微生物单细胞RT-qPCR和全转录组分析技术；二）作为技术的可行性证明，将应用这些技术对海洋光合蓝细菌进行研究, 实现未经培养微生物的单细胞全转录组分析；三）构建海洋低光环境中光合蓝细菌的基因网络，发现蓝细菌在典型大海洋生态环境中的代谢新途径及新调控机制。相关技术的开发将为水圈环境中其他重要微生物在地球元素循环中的意义研究提供重要的技术手段。"	"For functional analysis of microbes in the hydrosphere, two major challenges need to be overcome: 1) 99% of microbes in nature are unculturable; 2) understanding derived from laboratory-based pure_culture studies may not represent microbes in nature well enough. To address the issues, we propose to develop single-cell gene expression analysis technologies to study cyanobacteria in the hydrosphere. The specific aims are: 1) developing single-cell RT-PCR and single-cell transcriptomics to analyze gene expression in microbial single cells directly without cultivation; 2) as a proof of concept, the technologies developed under this proposal will be applied to the analysis of ocean cyanobacteria; 3) constructing the gene expression network of cyanobacteria under low-light environments in deep sea for deciphering new metabolic and regulatory mechanisms. Once executed, the study will establish the most needed technologies for the research community of microbes in hydrosphere. Meanwhile, the study on cyanobacteria will provide important insights on marine microbial ecology, ocean carbon sink and global carbon cycling."	
碳酸盐型盐湖碳硫元素循环的微生物驱动机制及适应机制	91751201	微生物代谢 ( C010204 )	向华	研究员	中国科学院微生物研究所	294.00万元	重大研究计划	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2021 年 12 月 31 日	微生物群落；嗜盐菌；元素循环；生理代谢；环境适应	Microbial community;Halophiles;Element cycling;Physiological metabolism;Environmental adaptation	碳酸盐型盐湖含有高浓度碳酸钠和其它一些可溶性盐类（如硫酸钠等），在全球干旱和半旱地区（如我国内蒙古高原）广泛分布。该类高盐高pH盐湖尽管环境苛刻，却孕育了丰富的微生物类群，其初级生产力效率甚至可达全球湖泊和流域平均水平的十多倍，在含盐含碱水生生境元素循环中发挥了独特的作用。本项目将基于申请人在嗜盐微生物代谢领域的长期积累，进一步聚焦于碳酸盐型盐湖及其功能微生物组，重点开展该特殊水生生境中碳硫元素循环的微生物驱动机制及其适应机制的研究。拟通过创新性培养技术和非培养策略，结合现代分子生物学方法，从微生物群落，关键功能菌株，特殊代谢途径，互作网络到适应机制等多个层次，系统揭示该类盐湖微生物参与碳硫元素循环的生理代谢机制及其分子基础，探讨碳硫元素循环策略对盐湖微生物特殊群落结构形成的贡献和对盐湖演化的可能影响，并为国家生态健康与环境安全（如含盐碱废水/含硫废气治理等）提供新的微生物资源与技术策略。	"The soda lakes are characterized by high concentrations of sodium carbonate and other dissolved salts，such as sodium chloride and sodium sulfate, and are widespread in arid and semi-arid areas of the earth (e.g. the Inner Mongolia plateau). Despite the harsh haloalkaline conditions, these lakes are usually inhabited by abundant microbial communities and are often highly productive, with gross primary production rates much higher than the global average for lakes and streams, thus the microbiota in the soda lakes would have played an important role in biogeochemical cycling of elements in such extreme aquatic environments. This project will focus on the carbonate-sulfate containing soda lakes, and concentrate on the microbe-driven carbon and sulfur cycling, as well as their environmental adaptation mechanisms in this unique saline system. By means of innovative culture methods, high-throughput culture-independent approaches and molecular biology techniques, we will reveal the mechanisms of the microbe-driven element cycling at levels of microbial community, functional strains, interaction networks, specific metabolic pathways and the related adaptation mechanisms. This project will systematically answer the scientific questions on microbial ecophysiological metabolism related to carbon and sulfur cycling, and provide novel insights into the microbial diversity in the soda lakes and its role in biogeochemistry and biomineralization. The achievements from this project will not only help to understand the microbial geochemical cycling of carbon and sulfur, but may also provide microbial resources and biotechnological potentials for supporting the national ecological health and environmental safety."	
基于微生物菌群变化的半夏曲发酵炮制增效作用机制研究	81773901	中药炮制 ( H2805 )	杨鸣华	副教授	中国药科大学	55.00万元	面上项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2021 年 12 月 31 日	半夏曲；炮制增效；物质基础；微生物菌群变化；止咳化痰	Pinelliae Rhizoma Fermentata ;synergetic Processing;material basis;microflora variation;relieving cough and reducing sputum	半夏曲的发酵炮制作用机制不清楚、物质基础不明确制约其合理有效的开发利用，而多菌种自然发酵的随机性是导致这一现状的关键问题之一。项目前期研究发现半夏块茎内生微生物菌群是发酵炮制的菌种来源，且炮制过程对菌群有定向筛选作用；亦证明发酵炮制后的半夏曲化学成分更丰富，微生物的生物转化和自身代谢产物极有可能发挥炮制增效作用。故创新性的以微生物菌群变化为切入点来研究发酵炮制后的活性物质基础变化，能够揭示半夏曲发酵炮制作用机制，阐明其发酵过程的科学内涵。基于此，本项目拟综合运用菌株分离鉴定和高通量测序技术，全面分析半夏曲发酵炮制过程中微生物菌群的变化，确定发酵优势菌群；结合生物活性筛选，从微生物的生物转化作用及自身代谢产物两方面发现发酵前后药效成分的区别，明确发酵增效的活性物质基础。本项目的开展有助于阐明半夏曲发酵炮制的科学意义，亦可为同类型发酵炮制中药的研究提供新的思路与方法，具有重要的理论和学术价值。	"The fermentation mechanism of Pinelliae Rhizoma Fermentata processing remaines a puzzler for us, which along with the unclear material basis, have restricted us from well developing of this traditional medicine. The randomness of natural fermentation is indeed a critical issue causing current situation. Our previous research revealed that the endophytic microflora from Pinellia tuber should be responsible for the fermentation which conversely sifted the microflora for itself. We also proved that the fermentation processing could produce more abundant chemical constituents through the bioconversion and second metabolism of microflora. More importantly, the newly generated constituents could provide Pinelliae Rhizoma Fermentata with synergistic effect. Therefore, the innovative research beginning by uncovering the microflora changes would be a breakthrough to reveal both the bioactive material basis and the fermentation mechanism of Pinelliae Rhizoma Fermentata processing. For further investigation, a comprehensive analysis of changes happened in process would lead us to the dominant microflora, which followed by researching the bioconversion and second metabolism of microflora, would make us to find the different bioactive products and to figure out the synergistic effect. So we launch this project to clarify the scientific significance in fermentation processing of Pinelliae Rhizoma Fermentata, and also to provide new ideas and methods for studying the similar fermented traditional Chinese Medicine. In conclusion, it’s a basic research project with important theoretical and academic value."

水环境中亚硝胺前体物的微生物代谢来源机制假说的验证研究	21777079	水污染化学 ( B060103 )	陈超	副研究员	清华大学	64.00万元	面上项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2021 年 12 月 31 日	亚硝胺；前体物；微生物代谢；氨基酸；含氮有机物	nitrosamine;precursor;microogranism metabolism;amino acids;nitrogeneous organic compounds	亚硝胺是一类新兴消毒副产物，在我国不少地区的饮用水中被普遍检出且风险较高。控制亚硝胺首先要识别其前体物的来源。但是国内外现有研究只能解释亚硝胺前体物的部分来源。申请人首次提出了微生物代谢可能是水中亚硝胺前体物重要来源的假说。本申请的目的就是要验证这一假说。主要内容包括：1.设计加工微生物培养反应器，投加典型氨基酸作为底物，接种典型菌种或混合菌种，检测代谢过程中的亚硝胺生成潜能变化。2.选择内容1培养时有高亚硝胺潜能的氨基酸，采购15N同位素标记氨基酸作为底物，用气相/液相色谱串联质谱、飞行时间质谱等多种手段检测培养过程中的各种代谢成分，梳理氨基酸代谢过程中的反应途径，确定亚硝胺前体物的产生机制。3.选择氨基酸浓度高的实际水体，进行上述机制的验证。项目研究成果将证实微生物代谢生成亚硝胺前体物的新模式，有助于评估微生物代谢对实际水体中亚硝胺及其前体物的贡献，指导建立保护水质安全措施。	"N-Nitrosamines (NAs) are a group of carcinogenic emerging disinfection by-products (DBPs). They present high risk to drinking water safety in many regions around China due to high occurrence and concentration. The first key step to control NAs is to identify the sources of their precursors. However, the recent knowledge about that cannot explain the majority of NA precursor sources. The applicant first propose a hypothesis on NA precursor formation from microorganism metabolism in aquatic environment. The aim of this application for NSFC project is to verify this hypothesis..The main tasks for this project include: (1) Design and make the specific incubators for this microorganism metabolism study, add the representative individual amino acid as the sole substrates, then inoculate the typical pure bacteria strains or mixture. Monitor the NA formation potential during the incubation termly as well as other water quality parameters. (2) Choose those amino acids with high NA formation potential change during the incubation on task 1, purchase the 15N-labelled certain amino acids as the substrate, analyze the products during the incubation by GC/LC-MS-MS, TOF-MS. Then, the pathway of amino acids metabolism could be recognized and the mechanism of NA precursors could be determined. (3) This mechanism would be verified by the study of incubating real water samples with high amino acid concentration..The results of this project will verify the new formation mechanism of NA and precursors via microorganism metabolism. It will help assess the contribution of NAs and precursors from microorganism in real aquatic environment and guide the measure development to protect water safety."	
东亚传统食品发酵剂中微生物相互作用及分子功能的比较宏基因组学分析研究	31711540295	食品微生物学基础 ( C200301 )	韩北忠	教授	中国农业大学	15.00万元	国际(地区)合作与交流项目	2017 年 07 月 01 日 至 2019 年 06 月 30 日	互作；功能；宏基因组学；大曲	Interactons;Functions;Metagenomics;Daqu	在东亚地区，人们利用中国大曲及韩国Nuruk等发酵剂来制作酒精饮料的历史悠久。中国的大曲作为白酒和食醋的发酵剂对产品质量和风味至关重要。韩国的Nuruk是一种用于米酒（Makgeolli）酿造的传统发酵剂。低温大曲以及Nuruk在制作原料、制作工艺等方面高度相似。本项目将采用宏基因组学方法对微生物群落进行物种注释和功能注释，利用COG， KEGG 和 CAZy等数据库对基因功能、代谢通路进行注释分析，结合物种多样性和功能多样性进行相关性分析、共现性分析及Network网络分析，总结发酵剂群落中微生物相互作用模式，采用全基因组测序及比较基因组学对发酵剂中优势且具有功能的真菌进行功能验证。建立混合微生物群落研究模型，并对功能真菌资源进行深度开发利用，以揭示东亚地区传统发酵剂的作用机制，提高东亚传统发酵剂以及发酵食品的国际影响力。	"In East Asia, various traditional fermentation starters are used to produce alcoholic beverages for centuries such as Daqu in China and Nuruk in South Korea. Daqu is a specific fermentation starter that plays a significant role in the production of Chinese liquor and vinegar. And Nuruk is a traditional natural starter, which is extensively used in the brewing of a traditional Korean alcoholic beverage called Makgeolli. The raw materials and production process of Nuruk are quite similar with Daqu especially low-temperature Daqu. Thus the function richness and microbial interactions of fermentation starters in East Asia will be revealed by metagenomics. Database such as COG, KEGG and CAZy will be used for the functional annotation and pathway mapping of metagenomes to better understand the functional potential and dominant species in microbial communities. Correlation, co-occurrence and network analysis will be conducted by combining the results of microbial diversity and functional diversity to determine the dominant species and its interaction patterns. Function-related genes of dominant fungi will be analyzed using whole genome sequencing and comparative genomics. This study can establish a model of microbial community for the research of interspecies interactions. And it can also get a deep insight into the mechanism of East Asia fermentation starters to improve international influence of East Asia fermentation starters and fermented food."	
壳聚糖对山药连作障碍的消减及对其根际微生物的调节	31760365	其他作物栽培学 ( C130306 )	张荣萍	副教授	海南大学	37.00万元	地区科学基金项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2021 年 12 月 31 日	经济作物；抗逆性；壳聚糖；消减；根际微生物	economic crops;resistance;chitosan;prevention;rhizosphere microorganisms	山药连作时病虫害多发，减产严重，表现出明显的连作障碍，严重影响了山药的品质和经济效益，生物有机肥措施可一定程度地改善根际微生物种群，减轻山药连作障碍，但目前的防治效果还不理想。前期研究表明，连作病害的病情指数与根际微生物种群结构关系密切。壳聚糖广泛存在于海洋生物虾蟹的外壳中，可调节根际微生物种群和生物酶活性，提高花生、香蕉、番木瓜、苹果和烟草等作物的抗逆性，减轻连作障碍和各种病害，且安全、便捷、环保。高通量测序技术能全面、准确、快速地反映微生物群落的组成、丰度。因此，本项目拟借助MiSeq高通量测序技术，研究壳聚糖对山药连作障碍的消减及对其根际微生物群落结构的调节，揭示根际微生物群落结构与病情指数和土壤理化生物性状之间的关系和壳聚糖消减山药连作障碍的根际微生物机理，探明健康山药根际微生物区系的标准及壳聚糖调控方法。	"When Yam plants were cropped continiously, diseases and insect pests occured significantly, yield discreased greatly which is named by continuous cropping obstacle, which is bad for yam developping high efficiently and sustainably. The way of biological organic fertilizer can improve the rhizosphere microorganisms, reduce yam continuous cropping obstacle to some extent, but the control effect is still not ideal. Previous research showed that,  disease index is closely related to rhizosphere microorganisms community. Chitosan is widespread in Marine biological shell of shrimp, crab, it could adjust rhizosphere microorganisms and enzyme activities, increase crop resistance to disease, reduce all kinds of diseases including continuous cropping obstacle. At the same time, chitosan is safe, convenient and environment friendly. The misequencing technology can analyze microbial community, abundance comprehensively and accurately. So, this project would use misequencing technology to study the prevention of continuous cropping obstacle and regulation of rhizosphere microorganisms by chitosan in yam, would reveal the relationship between rhizosphere microorganisms and disease index, physical and chemical properties, enzyme activity in soil, and the microorganism machanism of chitosan reducing yam continuous cropping obstacle, build soil microorganism standards for health yam rhizosphere microflora and its regulation method by chitosan."	
土地利用变化背景下凋落物分解与微生物群落之间相互作用机制的研究	31770563	土壤物质循环过程生态学 ( C031101 )	程晓莉	研究员	中国科学院武汉植物园	62.00万元	面上项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2021 年 12 月 31 日	凋落物分解；生态计量化学；土地利用变化；微生物群落组成；酶活性	Litter decomposition ;Ecological stoichiometry;Land use change;Microbial community composition ;Enzymatic activity	凋落物分解与微生物群落之间的相互作用机制是当代全球变化与生态系统碳氮循环研究的前沿问题。由于凋落物分解过程的复杂性和微生物多样性的特点，在土地利用变化背景下，凋落物分解与微生物之间如何相互作用有待于从机制层面进一步探究。本研究选择了丹江口水库库区不同土地利用类型（森林，灌丛和农田）为研究对象，通过野外和室内的凋落物交互移植实验，利用分子生物学技术（酶活性、PLFA和Illumina高通量测序），并结合元素分析和凋落物分解模型，研究凋落物分解与微生物群落之间的内在联系和相互作用过程。通过分析研究不同土地利用类型下凋落物质量和土壤理化性质的差异，揭示凋落物质量自身和土壤因素对凋落物分解速率和微生物群落组成的影响机制；通过分析凋落物分解过程中凋落物质量的变化与微生物群落组成之间的关系，揭示凋落物分解与微生物群落之间相互作用机制。本项目将为揭示生态系统碳氮循环对全球变化的响应机制提供科学依据。	"The mechanism of interaction between litter decomposition and microbial community is a frontier issue in contemporary global change and ecosystem carbon and nitrogen cycling research. Due to the complexity of the litter decomposition process and the characteristics of microbial diversity, the interaction between litter decomposition and microbial community needs to be further explored from the mechanism level under land use change. In this project, the different types of land use (woodland, shrubland and cropland) in Danjiangkou reservoir area will be selected as the research object, based on the field and indoor litter interactive transplant experiment, the relationship between litter decomposition and microbial community will be identified by using elemental analysis, litter decomposition model and technology of molecular biology (enzyme activity, PLFA and llumina high-throughput sequencing). By analyzing the differences of litter quality and soil physical and chemical properties under different land use types, the effects of litter quality and soil factors on litter decomposition rate, microbial community and function will be revealed. Based on the analysis of the relationship between litter decomposition and microbial community structure and function, the interaction mechanism between litter decomposition and microbial community will be clarified. This study provides the scientific theory for terrestrial ecosystem carbon and nitrogen cycling related to global environment change."	
基于功能性状的土壤微生物群落构建对林冠层氮沉降的响应	31700383	森林生态学 ( C030602 )	张晓	讲师	河南大学	26.00万元	青年科学基金项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2020 年 12 月 31 日	土壤微生物；基因组学；群落构建；微生物功能性状；林冠层氮沉降	Soil microbes;Genomics;Community assembly;Microbial functional traits;Canopy nitrogen deposition	群落构建机制是理解物种共存和多样性变化的核心问题，然而相关研究多集中于动植物领域，微生物的群落构建机制尚处于探索阶段。氮沉降是全球变化的一个重要方面，了解氮沉降背景下土壤微生物群落构建对准确预测森林生态系统如何调节和应对未来环境变化尤为重要。本项目拟借助国内首个“林冠模拟氮沉降”野外控制实验平台，利用高通量测序、宏基因组技术和生物信息学方法，从参与土壤生态过程的功能基因水平鉴定微生物功能性状对氮沉降的响应，研究林冠和林下模拟氮沉降处理下土壤微生物功能性状的变化规律，揭示对氮沉降响应敏感的关键功能性状；探讨环境筛和随机过程在氮沉降下微生物群落重建过程中的相对作用，阐明微生物群落构建对氮沉降的响应模式，从而为辨识全球变化对土壤微生物多样性及其生态功能的作用机制提供科学依据，也为建立森林生态学的土壤微生物群落构建理论体系作出贡献。	"Community assembly mechanisms have been the central issues of understanding species coexistence and diversity changes. Most previous studies focus on plant and animal communities, however, community assembly of microbial communities are poorly documented. Nitrogen (N) deposition is an important aspect of global change. Studying the response of assembly processes in soil microbial communities to N deposition is essential to predict how forest ecosystem adapts to environmental changes. Here, high-throughput sequencing, metagenome and bioinformatics methods will be used to study the responses of soil microbial functional traits to N deposition based on Canopy Addition N experiment in two forests in central and southern China. By analysing the responses of microbial functional traits to canopy and understory nitrogen addition, the sensitive microbial functional traits to N deposition will be ensured. The relative importance of environmental filtering and random effect in the community assembly processes will be disentangled, and response patterns of community assembly to N deposition will be detected. Our study will provide scientific basis to identify the mechanisms of biodiversity and ecological function of soil microorganisms to respond global changes and will contribute to preliminary microbial community assembly theories for forest ecology．"	
青藏高原高寒草甸毒草根际微生物多样性对草地退化的影响机制研究	31700396	草地与荒漠生态学 ( C030603 )	韩瑾	讲师	兰州大学	24.00万元	青年科学基金项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2020 年 12 月 31 日	土壤微生物；高通量测序；高寒草甸毒杂草；草地退化；根际微生物多样性	Soil Microbe ;High-throughput sequencing;Noxious weeds in Alpine meadow;Grassland degradation;Diversity of rhizosphere microbe	我国是一个草原大国，如何防护有害植物大量生长对于青藏高原草地优良牧草的可持续利用，草地植被的保护和草地生态系统的稳定有着重要的经济和战略意义。本项目以青藏高原草地易入侵的毒草黄帚橐吾(Ligularia virgaurea)为研究对象，紧紧围绕毒杂草根际微生物对草地退化的影响机制这一科学问题，全面比较同一生境下优良牧草（嵩草）和毒草（黄帚橐吾）根际微生物群落结构和多样性差异、营养循环利用关键基因的丰度及表达活性的差异，阐明毒草根际微生物在植被群落建成中的作用；并结合根系分泌物组成与根周土壤特性，探索草地生态系统中根际微生物群落与根际微环境之间的相互作用机制及其动态变化过程，为退化草地恢复技术的发展和草地植物根际微生物资源的合理利用方面具有重要的理论意义和实践价值。	"China is a grassland country with almost half of its total areas covered by various types of grassland plant species. Prevented noxious plants massive growth has far-reaching economic of political significance on sustainable utilization of fine pasture and protection of vegetation communities and stability of grassland ecosystem on Qinghai-Tibetan Plateau. This project focused on a noxious plant--Ligularia virgaurea, which was dominant species since grassland degeneration. We research the mechanism of plant＆rhizosphere microorganisms. We want to explain the relationship between noxious weeds community and rhizosphere microorganisms by finding out the differences between pastue (Kobresia Willd.) and noxious weeds(Ligularia virgaurea) on composition, diversity of rhizosphere microorganisms and the abundance and expression of nutrient cycle key genes. To explore the interactive mechanism of rhizosphere microorganisms’ community with rhizosphere micro-environment; as well as dynamic change by integrated with characteristic of root exudate and rhizosphere soil. We can provide more valuable information about degenerative grassland recovery and resources rational utilization of rhizosphere microorganisms."	
生物炭对桉树人工林酸性土壤N2O排放的影响及微生物响应机制	31760162	微生物生理生态学 ( C030303 )	徐广平	副研究员	广西壮族自治区中国科学院广西植物研究所	35.00万元	地区科学基金项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2021 年 12 月 31 日	硝化；反硝化；氨氧化微生物；真菌；稳定同位素示踪	Nitrification; Denitrification;Ammonia-oxidizing microorganisms;Fungi;Stable isotopic tracer	目前我国桉树人工林土壤出现酸化现象，加剧了酸性土壤N2O的排放。土壤硝化作用与反硝化作用通常耦合发生，氨氧化细菌，氨氧化古菌和真菌都有可能在酸性土壤硝化作用中起重要作用，其反应机制及其对N2O排放的贡献还需进一步明确。生物炭在减缓土壤N2O排放等方面有重要的作用，生物炭调控下，识别桉树人工林酸性土壤N2O排放的来源途径及微生物响应机制，对于桉树人工林N2O减排具有重要意义。该研究以广西桉树人工林酸性土壤为研究对象，开展生物炭(前期桉树废弃物制备)施用试验，通过静态箱―气相色谱法，结合气压过程分离法(BaPS)和稳定性同位素技术(δ15N，δ18O)，探讨土壤N2O的排放特征及来源途径；借助实时荧光定量PCR等现代分子生物学手段，揭示生物炭对土壤氨氧化微生物群落结构的影响，通过底物诱导呼吸抑制法和15N自然丰度，阐明真菌在土壤N2O排放的相对贡献，旨在为桉树人工林可持续经营提供科学依据。	"The soil acidification of Eucalyptus plantation in the southern Chinese province was obvious recently,which aggravated soil nitrous oxide (N2O) emissions in acidic Eucalyptus plantation to some extent. Soil nitrification and denitrification is usually occurring simultaneously.The mechanism of microbe and its contribution to N2O emissions need to be studied further because that ammonia oxidizing bacteria(AOB),ammonia oxidizing archaea(AOA) and fungi may all play an important role in nitrification of acid soil. Wastes from forestry is an ideal material for biochar,which are helpful to reduce soil N2O emissions etc. It is important for us to explore the source of soil N2O emission and microbial transformation in Eucalyptus plantation under the regulatory role of biochar addition especially now. On the basis of our previous research ,we already had some biochar that were made from forestry waste of Eucalyptus plantation. Therefore, a biochar addition control experiment will be designed in Eucalyptus plantation acid soil in Guangxi province, which were the largest district of Eucalyptus plantations in China. Effects of biochar on soil N2O emission will be measured by the static chamber-gas chromatography method. The contributions of nitrification and denitrification to soil N2O emission will be calculated by the barometric process separation (BaPS) method and stable isotope techniques (δ15N，δ18O) . At the same time, the key processes and microbial mechanisms of biochar on soil N2O emission were also studied through modern molecular biology methods, such as real time fluorescence quantitative PCR, DNA sequencing and phylogenetic analysis ,and so on.The relative contribution of fungi to soil N2O emission was determinated by substrate induced respiration and 15N natural abundance method respectively. These results will provide some information for applying biochar to reduce soil N2O emission in forest production. The scientific data for the forest sustainable management policy would be suggested for Eucalyptus Plantation."	
基于多组学技术的原料乳冷藏过程中微生物群落演替驱动机制研究	31760479	畜产食品贮藏与保鲜 ( C200604 )	剧柠	副教授	宁夏大学	38.00万元	地区科学基金项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2021 年 12 月 31 日	乳；品质；微生物群落演替；驱动机制；多组学技术	milk;quality;Microbial community succession;Driving mechanism;Multiple omics technology	优质原料乳是生产高品质乳制品的前提，宁夏是农业部确定的全国奶牛优势区，是重要的优质奶源基地。冷藏可以有效降低原料乳中微生物的生长。但其缓慢生长及产生的酶类物质仍会造成原料乳及乳制品的品质劣变。目前国内外原料乳微生物的研究着眼于生物多样性、腐败菌及嗜冷菌的特性研究及检测，对冷藏过程中乳成分变化导致的微生物群落演替及其腐败机制的相关生态学领域未做深入研究。项目拟采用基于SMRT的宏基因组学技术结合选择培养法研究原料乳冷藏过程中微生物群落演替规律，采用基于iTRAQ的宏蛋白质组学技术、采用基于UPLC-Q-TOF-MS的代谢组学技术研究群落演替与营养、代谢组份及环境条件变化的关系，研究基因、蛋白质及其分子间相互作用，通过构建基因互作网络、蛋白质互作网络、代谢网络，经多组学关联，揭示微生物群落演替的内在驱动机制。为原料乳冷藏的质量控制层次的提供深理论依据，为冷藏技术创新提供理论参考。	"High quality of raw milk is the premise of good dairy products. Ningxia is the national dairy advantage region which was determined by The Ministry of agriculture and is also the important high quality milk source base of china.  Refrigeration can effectively reduce microbial propagation speed. But, in low temperature, raw milk and milk products also can be deteriorated by the microorganisms growing slowly and the enzyme they produce. In recent years, researchers in the world pay more attention to analysis the biodiversity, characte and detecte the dominant spoilage strains in raw milk. However, scholars did not do indepth research on microbial ecology on the changes of milk components leading to the microbial community succession and corruption mechanism in raw milk. Using the techniques of metagenomics based on SMRT with dependent cultivation methods, the microorganism community succession will be studied. Using the techniques of proteinomics based on iTRAQ and metabolomics based on UPLC-Q-TOF-MS, the relationship among microorganism community succession, nutrition, metabolism and the environmental conditions will be studied. Through building the gene interactions network, the protein interaction network and the metabolic networkthe, associating the multiple omics, the inner driving mechanism of microbial community succession on raw milk during refrigeration will be constructed. The study aims to provide an indepth theory basis for the quality control of raw milk, and it will provide a theoretical reference for the renovation of the refrigerated technology."	
低盐发酵酸鱼典型产胺微生物促生物胺形成机制研究	31760455	食品发酵 ( C200303 )	曾雪峰	讲师	贵州大学	38.00万元	地区科学基金项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2021 年 12 月 31 日	发酵；细菌微生物；酸鱼；生物胺；氨基酸脱羧酶	fermentation;microbial;Suan yu;biogenic amines;decarboxylase	低盐发酵酸鱼是我国西南少数民族地区一种传统的发酵水产品，但由于该产品低盐、易污染微生物、易产酸及富含游离氨基酸的特点，为生物胺的合成提供了良好的条件。然而，目前对低盐发酵酸鱼生物胺的形成机理研究还很缺乏。本研究以贵州传统低盐发酵酸鱼为研究对象，重点考察发酵过程中微生物种类、数量对生物胺形成的影响，通过对筛选获得的典型产胺微生物产胺性能，降解及控制生物胺分析，再通过对典型产胺菌株氨基酸脱羧酶基因克隆表达，对获取的重组蛋白及分离的氨基酸脱羧酶的酶学性质及结构研究，以求从微生物和基因层面探讨影响低盐发酵酸鱼生物胺的形成机制。本研究对于揭示低盐发酵酸鱼生物胺的形成机理，为确定控制酸鱼生物胺技术、建立工业化生产酸鱼制品提供一定的理论基础。	"Low-salt fermented Suan yu is a traditional fermented aquatic product in the minority nationalities of south-western China, extensively produced  acid, rich in free amino acid and prone to being contaminated by bacteria due to low-salt, which provides favorable conditions for synthesis of biogenic amines. However, at present, the formation and accumulation mechanism of biogenic amines in low-salt fermented Suan yu therein still remain undefined. With the traditional low-salt fermented Suan yu as the research object, the effect of species and quantities of microorganisms of the Suan yu fermentation process, and biodegradation and control of biogenic amines were analyzed. Through selection typical microbial producing biogenic amine, investigation the ability producing biogenic amines. Through cloning, expression and enzyme character of amino acid decarboxylase from low-salt fermented Suan yu, and research of the properties and structure of obtaining recombinant protein and the separation of amino acid decarboxylase enzymology. Thus study the formation of biogenic amines in Suan yu from the aspects of microorganism and genetic level. The research offers a certain theoretical foundation for revealing formation mechanism of biogenic amines, determining the technique of biogenic amine control in low-salt fermented Suan yu, and industrializing the Suan yu products eventually."	
入侵生物马铃薯甲虫肠道微生物对寄主植物抗虫防御的调控及其机理	31701855	植物检疫与生物入侵 ( C1407 )	王杰	讲师	福建农林大学	25.00万元	青年科学基金项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2020 年 12 月 31 日	入侵昆虫；扩散机制；马铃薯甲虫；肠道微生物；寄主防御	invasive insect;diffusion mechanism;Colorado potato beetle;gut microbes;host defense	马铃薯甲虫是国际公认的马铃薯毁灭性害虫，入侵我国新疆地区后，对我国马铃薯产业构成了严重的威胁，且其进一步扩散的风险正在加剧。肠道微生物是昆虫重要的组成部分，与宿主昆虫相互合作、协同进化。课题组前期研究表明，肠道微生物参与调控了植物的抗虫性，但目前还不知道其是否介导马铃薯甲虫的生物入侵。本项目拟以入侵我国的马铃薯甲虫为主要研究对象，利用16S rRNA扩增子测序、宏基因组测序以及传统培养法对其肠道微生物进行分离鉴定，分析比较美国原产地与入侵地新疆马铃薯甲虫肠道微生物种类和丰度的差异，测定肠道差异菌株对马铃薯植株抗虫能力和防御反应的影响，再利用荧光原位杂交技术和荧光定量PCR技术验证肠道差异菌株存在的部位和含量，从而揭示肠道微生物可能协助马铃薯甲虫在新的入侵地适应寄主植物抗性加剧生物入侵的机制，进一步阐明昆虫生物入侵机制和昆虫肠道微生物的生态学功能，为入侵生物马铃薯甲虫的综合防控提供新的策略。	"Colorado potato beetle (CPB, Leptinotarsa decemlineata) is a very important destructive pest worldwide. After its invasion to Xinjiang Autonomous Region this pest has caused huge losses of potato yield together with the increasing risk of further dispersal and spreading to inland. Gut-associated microbes are treated as significant organs of insects, and interact and co-evolve with their host-insects. Our previous work showed that gut microbes played a key role in regulating plant induced defenses, but there is little information about the role of gut-associated microbes in the manipulation of invasive process of CPB. This study will investigate the gut microbes of invasive CPB using the methods of 16S rRNA sequencing, metagenome analysis and traditional bacterial isolation and identification. We will compare the differences in the diversity and abundance of gut microbes of CPB colonies between the native region United States and introduced region Xinjiang, and figure out the distinct bacterial isolates. Then the function of these different bacterial isolates in mediating the resistance and induced defenses of potato plants to insects will be determined. Fluorescence in situ hybridization will be used to observe the location of target bacterial strains, and the relative quantities of these bacteria on leaves or in insect inner organ will be examined by quantitative real time PCR. This study will test the hypothesis whether or not the gut-associated microbes play a key role in assisting CPB to adapt to the host-plant defense system to facilitate its invasion to new regions. The results will highlight the novel mechanism of CPB invasion and  important ecological role of gut microbes, thus will provide a new guideline for invasive pest management."	
猪肠道微生物区系-代谢物-宿主肌内脂肪沉积的相互调控机制	31760645	畜禽性状形成的基础 ( C170101 )	赵素梅	教授	云南农业大学	40.00万元	地区科学基金项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2021 年 12 月 31 日	种质资源；肉质性状；猪；肠道微生物；肌内脂肪沉积	germplasm resource;meat quality;pig;intestinal microflora;intramuscular fat deposition	大河乌猪具有肌内脂肪含量高的种质特性，是制作云南高原特色畜产品―宣威火腿的原料。大河乌猪肌内脂肪含量高的种质特性必然与其肠道微生物密切相关。本项目拟以大河乌猪为试验材料，以长白猪为对照，首先测定背最长肌肌内脂肪含量，利用HPGC检测回肠、空肠和盲肠各肠段短链脂肪酸含量，采用16S rRNA和宏基因组学测序比较大河乌猪与长白猪肠道微生物群落及基因功能差异，关联分析微生物区系-代谢物及肌内脂肪含量，筛选可能与肌内脂肪含量相关的微生物菌群及优势群落基因；利用real time PCR技术定量检测差异微生物群落基因丰度，从而阐明猪肠道微生物区系-代谢物及宿主肌内脂肪沉积间相互调控机制，该研究结果将丰富乌金猪肌内脂肪沉积的分子机制理论，为深度挖掘和高效利用乌金猪优良种质资源，开发安全、健康的畜产品提供理论依据，为通过营养措施调控肠道微生物，增加猪肌内脂肪沉积，改善猪肉品质，提供新的思路和可行的途径。	"Wujin pigs as Yunnan excellent local breeds with special characteristics of higher intramuscular fat content, is the raw material to produce Xuanwei ham. The traits of higher intramuscular fat content in Wujin pigs are closely related to the special intestinal microflora. On the basis of our previous studies and combined with the domestic and foreign research focus, The project intends to use Wujin pigs as experimental materials and Landrace as control. Intramuscular fat content was determined in Longissimus dorsi muscle. Fatty acid concentrate in different intestinal segment will be detected firstly by high pressure liquid chromatography (HPGC). Microbial flora diversity will be measured using 16S rRNA and metagenomic analysis technology. The different intestinal microflora between Wujin and Landrace pigs would be analyzed and to screen the microbial flora which may be associated with the content of metabolites and intramuscular fat. The abundance of microbial communities would be determined by real time PCR technology. The results of this study will enrich the molecular mechanism theory of intramuscular fat deposition in Wujin pig and provide the theoretical basis to mine and use Wujin pigs resources, to develop the safe, health of Yunnan plateau characteristics of animal products. The study would provide new ideas and feasible ways through nutrition regulation and control measures of gut microbes to increase porcine intramuscular fat deposition, improve meat quality."	
土壤微生物群落结构和多样性对玉米根茎叶分解过程的动态响应机制	41701330	土壤肥力与土壤养分循环 ( D070106 )	孙良杰	讲师	沈阳农业大学	23.00万元	青年科学基金项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2020 年 12 月 31 日	土壤培肥；土壤有机碳；稳定同位素技术；土壤微生物群落结构和多样性；玉米秸秆分解	soil fertility improvement;soil organic carbon;stable isotope tracing;soil microbial community structure and diversity;maize straw decomposition	由于玉米根茎叶中碳氮比和有机碳组成化学特性的差异性，还田后会导致土壤微生物群落及其主导的分解过程不同，因此弄清土壤微生物群落结构和多样性对其不同部位分解过程的动态响应是揭示秸秆还田提升土壤固碳与培肥能力机理的重要前提。本研究利用已获得的13C标记的玉米根茎叶为试材，通过室内培养试验开展以下研究：1）利用微生物磷脂脂肪酸技术结合高通量测序分析技术，分析玉米根茎叶分解不同时期的微生物群落结构及多样性，明确玉米根茎叶分解中微生物群落的响应变化过程；2）利用气相色谱―同位素比例质谱联用技术测定不同微生物类群磷脂脂肪酸δ13C值，区分新老有机碳的影响，分析玉米根茎叶分解过程中土壤微生物类群对新老有机碳的动态响应特征；3）综合分析微生物群落变化及其对新碳响应情况，最终阐明土壤微生物群落结构和多样性对玉米根茎叶分解过程的动态响应机制。本研究为秸秆还田作用下的土壤培肥机制提供理论基础及依据。	"Straw return is an effective measurement to improve soil fertility and carbon sequestration potential. Based on the hypothesis that the different plan tissues, with various C/N ratios and chemical composition of organic carbon, could influence their microbial decomposition, this research will focus on the response of microbial community and diversity to the decomposition process of root, stem and leaf of the 13C labeled maize through an incubation experiment, which is the key for us to understand the mechanism of soil fertility preservation and carbon fixation by straw return. A batch of incubation experiment will be set up with 13C-labeled maize plants, trying to achieve as follows: 1) Soil phospholipid fatty acid (PLFA), as well as bacterial and fungal gene diversity, analyzed by the method of high-throughput sequencing, will be analyzed to evaluate the dynamic changes of soil microbial community structure and diversity with decomposition of different tissues of maize. 2) Stable isotope labeling combined with phospholipid fatty acids analysis, with the help of GC-C-IRMS, will be used to assess who will be associated with the response of soil microbial groups to the tissues decomposition, the new organic matter (maize tissues) or the old one (soil organic matter). 3) The study will explicit the dynamic response mechanism of soil microbial community structure and diversity to the decomposition of maize root, stem and leaf, based on the combined analysis of microbial community changes and new organic matter utility. The proposed project will provide us with theory basis of soil fertility improvement in cropland under straw return."	
污水体系中微生物胞外聚合物对鸟粪石矿化的影响机制研究	41702034	矿物学（含矿物物理学） ( D0203 )	李涵	博士后	中国科学技术大学	27.00万元	青年科学基金项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2020 年 12 月 31 日	鸟粪石；胞外聚合物；成核作用；晶体生长；低温矿物合成	struvite;extracellular polymeric substances;nucleation;crystal growth;low-temperature mineral synthesis	从污水尤其是污泥水中结晶鸟粪石是氮磷回收的有效途径，但存在有机物干扰问题，这降低了鸟粪石结晶工艺的效率和回收产物的品质。已有的研究较少关注有机物对鸟粪石矿化的影响，这使得鸟粪石矿化处于“失控”状态。本项目选择污泥水中有机物的主要组分微生物胞外聚合物(EPS)开展鸟粪石矿化实验。通过分析EPS对鸟粪石成核和生长动力学的影响，了解EPS对鸟粪石结晶效率的影响机制。表征鸟粪石在EPS上的成核过程，揭示EPS调控鸟粪石成核的微观机制。考察EPS与鸟粪石晶面作用的方式和在鸟粪石上的赋存状态，揭示EPS调控鸟粪石形貌结构和掺杂鸟粪石的微观机制。研究EPS对鸟粪石表面电势的影响，查明EPS影响鸟粪石聚集和沉降的机制。研究EPS对鸟粪石溶解作用的影响，查明EPS促进鸟粪石溶解的方式和机制。成果的取得，有助于系统理解污泥水中EPS对鸟粪石矿化的影响，为发展鸟粪石结晶工艺提供实验矿物学上的指导。	"Struvite crystallization from wastewater especially reject water is an effective way to recover nitrogen and phosphorus, but there is an organic matter disturbance problem that reduces the efficiency of the crystallization process and the quality of the recovered product. The previous studies are less concerned about the impact of organic matter on struvite mineralization, making the struvite mineralization in the ""out of control"" state. This project will choose microbial extracellular polymeric substances (EPS), the main components of organic matter in the reject water, to carry out the struvite mineralization experiments. The impact of EPS on the nucleation and growth kinetics of struvite will be analyzed to understand the influence mechanism of EPS on the crystallization efficiency of struvite. The nucleation process of struvite on EPS will be characterized to reveal the microcosmic mechanism of EPS to control struvite nucleation. The mode of action between EPS and struvite surface and the occurrence state of EPS on struvite crystals will be investigated to reveal the microscopic mechanism of EPS controlling the morphology and structure of struvite and reducing struvite purity. The effect of EPS on the surface potential of struvite will be studied to find out the influence mechanism of EPS on the accumulation and deposition of struvite. The effect of EPS on struvite dissolution will be studied to find out the way and mechanism of EPS to promote struvite dissolution. The obtained results are helpful to systematically understand the effect of EPS on struvite mineralization in the reject water and provide guidance for the development of struvite crystallization process in experimental mineralogy."	
季节非对称性增温对高寒草甸植物与微生物养分关系的影响	41703079	生物地球化学 ( D0312 )	宗宁	助理研究员	中国科学院地理科学与资源研究所	24.00万元	青年科学基金项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2020 年 12 月 31 日	季节非对称性增温；冻融时期；植物-土壤关系；养分利用；后续效应	Seasonal asymmetric warming;Freezing-thawing events;Interactions between plant and soil microbes;Nutrient utilization;Carry-over effect	"青藏高原气候变暖呈现非生长季升温幅度高于生长季的季节非对称性升温趋势，导致冬春转换时期冻融循环提前、频率增加，将对受氮限制的高寒生态系统的养分循环产生重要影响。但当前的增温研究集中于全年增温的影响，忽略了季节非对称性升温的事实。为了阐明高寒生态系统对气候变化的响应及其机制，亟待研究季节非对称性升温对冻融时期植物与土壤微生物养分利用关系及其后续效应。本项目基于植物-微生物响应与作用的理论框架，在西藏当雄草原站季节非对称性增温试验平台，采用原位培养和15N同位素标记技术,动态监测季节非对称性升温对冻融时期微生物养分释放及植物养分吸收过程的影响，探讨微生物介导的资源供应变化如何影响生长季植物-微生物养分关系。项目结果有望为高寒生态系统养分循环对未来气候变化的响应提供机理解释。"	"Warming in winter on the Qinghai-Tibetan Plateau is over-proportionally affected by climate warming. The observed warming over the past decades is greater in non-growing season than in growing season. An increased frequency of soil freeze_thaw cycles at the winter-spring transition induced by warming during non-growing season may have great impacts on nutrient cycles in alpine ecosystems. However, studies on warming mostly focused on year-round warming effects, and ignored the facts of asymmetric warming. To better understand the response and underlying mechanism of alpine ecosystems to climate change, studies on the partitioning of nitrogen (N) between plants and soil microbes at the winter-spring transition and carry-over effects are needed. Based on field asymmetric warming experiment, we will dynamically monitor the N decoupling process during soil freezing-thaw cycles using in-suit incubation and 15N isotope tracer techniques in an alpine meadow. We will also investigate the carry-over effects on nutrient supply and the competition for N between plants and soil microbes during growing season. The results of this study are expected to provide insights into how nutrient cycling of alpine ecosystem responds to future climate change and its mechanism on the Qinghai-Tibetan Plateau."	
氯化乙烯原位微生物修复结合含水层储能系统中的生物地球化学行为	41703071	污染物行为过程及其环境效应 ( D0708 )	倪卓彪	副研究员	中山大学	24.00万元	青年科学基金项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2020 年 12 月 31 日	环境生物地球化学；原位生物修复；氯代烯烃；厌氧微生物；地下水污染	Environmental biogeochemistry;In-situ bioremediation;Chlorinated hydrocarbons;Anaerobic microorganism;Groundwater contamination	城市含水土层中氯化乙烯污染是普遍而严峻的环境问题，修复该污染的原位微生物修复技术ISB是国内外研究热点。然而ISB普遍周期长，效率亟需提高。基于同时解决环境与能源问题理念所提出的“ISB与清洁能源含水层储能系统（ATES）的结合技术”，是目前国际上备受关注的研究前沿。作为新型技术，相关的研究目前仍处于初期阶段，结合技术背后涉及的复杂生物地球化学行为尚未得到深入解释。本项目以探索结合体系间的相互影响为目的，拟开展高度模拟结合系统的土柱与批式机理性实验，探讨结合体系的局部与整体变化，并联合运用分析化学、分子生物学及环境微生物学技术，深究背后复杂的生物地球化学行为过程，阐明ATES（温度高低交替变化、地下水流极大增强）对氯化乙烯原位微生物修复的作用，明确相关厌氧微生物在此环境下的运动行为机理，并揭示微生物活动对ATES运行的潜在影响，以期为该结合技术的发展和未来成熟应用提供科学依据和技术支撑。	"Chlorinated ethenes (CVOCs) have been extensively used in the industrial sectors, especially in the dry-cleaning industry, leading to contamination of groundwater and risk of human health. As a cost-effective remediation technique, in-situ bioremediation (ISB) has been widely investigated and applied throughout the world for CVOCs remediation. However, the property of long duration of ISB might limit its further development and re-use of the contaminated land. To overcome this drawback, innovation or combination with other technology in a broader urban developing framework is needed. The combination of ISB and the novel sustainable energy technology -aquifer thermal energy storage (ATES)- could be a promising approach which might deal with environmental and energy problem simultaneously. Preliminary research has shown that the compatibility of these two is relatively high and ATES seems to have positive effects on ISB. By conducting series of batch and column experiments that highly mimic ATES-ISB system, and applying analytical chemistry, molecular microbiology and environmental microbiology techniques, this project focuses on investigate the related important biogeochemical processes in the combined system. We aim to clarify how ATES affects CVOCs bioremediation through by periodically changing temperature and highly enhancing groundwater movement; reveal how microorganisms behave under ATES condition; and determine the influence of microbial activities on ATES functioning. The outcome of this study is meaningful for the development of ATES-ISB technology and is expected to provide useful theoretical and practical guidelines."	
微生物胞外聚合物-锰氧化物微界面上铈分配异常的分子机制	41703119	环境地球化学 ( D0707 )	余茜倩	讲师	中国地质大学（武汉）	22.00万元	青年科学基金项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2020 年 12 月 31 日	锰氧化物；稀土元素；可溶性有机物；生物氧化锰；矿物界面反应	Mn oxide;REE;DOM;biogenic Mn oxide;Mineral interface reaction	微生物胞外聚合物(EPS)-锰氧化物与土壤溶液交界处形成的微界面是土壤中最活跃的反应位点之一，影响着稀土元素的富集和迁移。作为变价稀土元素，铈(Ce)在氧化锰表面的吸附氧化作用使其分布相对相邻稀土元素呈现正异常。前期研究发现，EPS可使Ce(IV)从氧化锰表面溶出，导致其在氧化锰表面呈现负异常。然而EPS与氧化锰耦合作用对Ce分配异常影响的分子机制仍不清楚。本项目选取EPS和氧化锰为研究对象，以EPS中常见的化学组分为对照，采用SEC-UV-ICP-MS联用技术、XAFS光谱技术等现代仪器分析手段，先获取二元体系下EPS分别与氧化锰和Ce的配位方式及络合容量；再分析三元体系下EPS及其关键组分对Ce化学形态及固液分配的影响；探究EPS与氧化锰的耦合作用对Ce异常值变化的影响机理。为合理解释表生环境中Ce异常分布变化的多样性提供理论依据，也为稀土及放射性核素污染土壤的修复和风险评价提供参考。	"The micro-interface between microbe extracellular polymeric substances (EPS)，Mn oxide, and soil solution is one of the most reactive sites in soil, which affect the accumulation and migration behavior of rare earth element (REE). As a redox sensitive REE, Ce(III) could be oxidized by Mn oxide to less soluble Ce(IV). Therefore, a positive Ce anomaly is commonly observed on Mn oxide. In previous studies, we found that EPS could induce the formation of a negative Ce anomaly on Mn oxide. However, the coupled effect of EPS and Mn oxide on Ce anomaly formation is still unclear. In this work, the EPS and Mn oxide are used as research objects, the main chemical compounds in EPS are used as model materials. A combination of SEC-UV-ICP-MS and XAFS spectroscopy is used to clarify 1) the binding characteristics and the complex capacity between EPS-Mn oxide and Ce-EPS in a binary system; and 2) the effect of EPS as well as its key chemical compounds on chemical species and distribution coefficient of Ce in a ternary system. The final goal is to explore the coupled effect of EPS and Mn oxide on Ce anomaly formation. This knowledge is vital for understanding the diversity of Ce anomaly distribution in aquatic and terrestrial environments, also helpful for the remediation and risk assessment of Ce and nuclear waste contaminated soil."	
拟穴青蟹血淋巴共生微生物菌群的代谢功能多样性研究	41706185	生物海洋学与海洋生物资源 ( D0604 )	张新旭	博士后	汕头大学	25.00万元	青年科学基金项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2020 年 12 月 31 日	拟穴青蟹；血淋巴；共生微生物；代谢功能；宏基因组	Scylla paramamosain;hemolymph;symbiotic microorganisms;metabolic function;metagenome	生活在宿主体内的微生物对宿主的免疫功能发挥着关键作用，是近年来生物学领域的研究热点之一。拟穴青蟹是我国东南沿海重要的海水养殖蟹类，申请人前期的研究发现，健康青蟹的血淋巴中含有共生微生物（包括弧菌、希瓦氏菌和气单胞菌），且其丰度比濒死和刚死亡的个体低4个数量级。血淋巴是青蟹免疫应答发生的主要场所，目前缺乏对青蟹血淋巴共生微生物的深入研究。本项目拟采用微生物生态学、宏基因组学及分子免疫学等手段揭示血淋巴共生微生物菌群的代谢功能多样性，来验证假说“血淋巴共生微生物拮抗外来微生物，血淋巴中含有潜在的病原菌，以及血淋巴共生微生物可以激活宿主的基础免疫”。通过本项目的研究，有助于揭示青蟹血淋巴共生微生物菌群抗病原菌感染的机理，丰富和完善无脊椎动物共生微生物与宿主相互作用的机制；在实践上有助于开发增强青蟹免疫力的微生物制剂及给药途径，来控制青蟹病害的发生与传播，对青蟹养殖业的疾病防治具有潜在的应用价值	"Symbiotic microorganisms play a key role in the host’s immunologic function, which is a research hotspot in recent years. The mud crab Scylla paramamosain is an important marine-derived aquacultured species in the southeast coast of China. Our previous results indicated the presence of symbiotic microorganisms in the hemolymph of healthy crabs (including Vibrio, Shewanella and Aeromonas), and the microbial abundances in the hemolymph of healthy crabs were approximately 4 orders of magnitude lower than those in moribund or dead ones. Despite the fact that hemolymph is a major site for host immune response, the functions of the symbiotic microorganisms in the hemolymph of S. paramamosain was less studied. This study aims to reveal the metabolic functional diversity of symbiotic microorganisms in the hemolymph of S. paramamosain, by combining the state-of-the-art techniques including microbial ecology, metagenomics and molecular immunology. This study would test the hypothesis that symbiotic hemolymph microorganisms may compete with incoming microorganisms, contain potential pathogens, and activate host basal immunity. This study would facilitate our understanding of the antibacterial function of symbiotic hemolymph microorganisms, and improve the knowledge of the microbe-host interactions in invertebrates. Meanwhile, this study gives clues to develop microbial immunoenhancer, and contributes to select appropriate administration routes for disease control, which would have potential applications in crab aquaculture"	
降水变化条件下荒漠草原土壤有机碳固持和稳定的微生物调控机制	41761043	环境变化与预测 ( D0710 )	张丽华	副教授	西北师范大学	40.00万元	地区科学基金项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2021 年 12 月 31 日	气候变化；环境效应；适应性；敏感性；脆弱性	climate change;environmental effect;adaptation;sensitivity;vulnerability	降水变化对土壤有机碳动态的影响及其机制是评估气候变化对陆地生态系统影响的关键科学问题之一。但现有研究关于荒漠草原土壤碳固存如何响应干旱和降水量增加仍旧尚未得出明确结论，对其响应机制亦不明确，严重阻碍了生态系统功能对气候变化响应的科学评估。本项目以黄土高原西部荒漠草原这一典型的气候敏感区为研究对象，通过野外控制试验模拟降水变化梯度，在团聚体尺度上分析土壤有机碳及其组分、土壤微生物群落组成、酶活性和基础呼吸对降水变化的响应，查明土壤微生物群落结构和功能改变的主控生境因子和驱动作用，揭示降水变化条件下土壤微生物群落结构和功能对土壤碳转化的调控路径，阐明降水改变对微生物调控土壤碳固持的影响机理，为科学评估全球气候变化背景下降水量改变对荒漠草原土壤碳源/汇功能的影响和土壤固碳潜力提供有力的实证数据。	"The impact and mechanism of precipitation change on soil organic carbon dynamic is one of key issues evaluating the impact of climate change on terrestrial ecosystems. However, there has been no definite conclusion and mechanism drawn from the response of soil carbon sequestration to reduced and increased precipitation, which seriously hinders the scientific assessment of responses of ecosystem function to climate change. The study area of this program lies in the desert steppe in the west of Loess Plateau, the typical climate sensitive area. Along the manipulated precipitation gradient of field control experiment, through analyzing the responses of soil organic carbon and its fractions, soil microbial community composition, enzyme activity and basal respiration at the aggregate scale to precipitation change, to find out the primary habitat factors and driving effect for the soil microbial community structure and function, to reveal the regulation pathway of soil microbial community structure and function on soil carbon transformation under the conditions of precipitation change, to illuminate the regulation mechanism of soil microbe on soil carbon sequestration, to provide powerful demonstration data for the scientific assessment of the influences of altered precipitation on the soil carbon source/sink function and soil carbon sequestration potential in the desert grassland under the background of global climate change."	
典型淡水养殖湿地甲烷和氧化亚氮排放及其关联微生物机制的比较研究	41771268	土壤化学 ( D070103 )	刘树伟	副教授	南京农业大学	63.00万元	面上项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2021 年 12 月 31 日	水产养殖湿地；温室气体；气候变化；增温潜势；排放系数	Aquaculture wetland;Greenhouse gas;Climate change;Global warming potential;Emission factor	农业淡水养殖湿地是大气甲烷（CH4）和氧化亚氮（N2O）重要排放源，其对全球变暖的贡献备受国内外学者关注。本项目针对当前我国淡水养殖模式多样和快速发展现状，以江苏地区代表性的淡水养殖湿地为研究对象，通过对典型单养、套养和混养淡水养殖湿地生态系统碳氮过程与CH4和N2O直接和间接排放的原位观测比较研究，项目将完成：（1）比较不同养殖湿地系统碳氮过程的周年和年际动态特征及驱动机制；（2）评估不同水产养殖系统CH4和N2O直接和间接排放强度及其一致性；（3）揭示典型养殖模式下湿地系统土壤碳氮与CH4和N2O排放的关联微生物驱动机制。研究结果将有助于完善我国湿地CH4和N2O排放清单编制，为寻求高效、生态和低碳的水产养殖模式提供科学依据。	"Aquaculture wetlands are important anthropogenic sources of atmospheric methane (CH4) and nitrous oxide (N2O), which have been gaining increasing attention among the governments and scientists worldwide. Based on the current diverse and rapid development status of aquaculture in China, this study will be carried out in aquaculture wetlands with typical culture models in Jiangsu area. By annual field measurements of CH4 and N2O fluxes from monoculture, polyculture and mixed-culture wetlands, the study will address the following concerns: (i) To compare the annual and interannual dynamics of ecosystem carbon and nitrogen processes by linking to their underlying mechanisms among aquaculture wetlands with different culture models. (ii) To evaluate the direct and indirect emission rates of CH4 and N2O among typical aquaculture wetlands. (iii) To reveal the soil microbial mechanisms associated with CH4 and N2O emissions in typical aquaculture wetland systems. Results of this study would be conducive to improve the compiling of national inventory of CH4 and N2O emissions from the overall wetlands in China, and simultaneously provide scientific basis and data support for seeking high-efficient, ecological and low-carbon aquaculture production models."	
土壤中邻苯二甲酸酯微生物降解的有机-矿质复合体界面作用机制	41771353	土壤污染与修复 ( D070107 )	罗斯	副教授	湖南农业大学	63.00万元	面上项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2021 年 12 月 31 日	邻苯二甲酸酯；界面行为；粘粒级有机-矿质复合体；吸附解吸；生物可降解性	PAEs;interface  behavior;clay organo-mineral complexes;sorption and desorption;biodegradability	邻苯二甲酸酯（PAEs）在土壤中的残留与污染已引起国内外广泛关注，正确预测其生物可降解性对于生态风险评估和农产品安全管理具有重要意义。目前就土壤中PAEs微生物降解与其在粘粒级有机-矿质复合体上界面行为的关系及机制还鲜见报道。本项目以自然土壤、粘粒级有机-矿质复合体及模拟有机-矿质复合体为吸附剂，在对其进行表面和结构特性表征的基础上，考察PAEs在各吸附剂上的界面行为，建立吸附剂的主要特征参数与吸附/解吸系数之间的相关关系；重点研究粘粒级有机-矿质复合体界面作用对土壤中PAEs微生物降解过程的影响，构建PAEs在土壤和粘粒级有机-矿质复合体中的生物可降解性与吸附/解吸系数间的理论模型，探讨土壤中不同形态PAEs的微生物降解性能，从而揭示影响PAEs微生物降解的主要因素，明确不同特性土壤中PAEs生物可降解性的差异机制。本研究有望为后续的PAEs污染控制技术和风险管理决策提供科学依据。	"The residues and contamination of phthalate esters (PAEs) in soils have attracted widely attention in the world. The correct prediction of PAEs biodegradability would pave a better way for risk assessment and management of PAEs contaminated sites and environmental health. However, studies about the interrelationships between the PAEs biodegradability and its interface behaviors on clay organo-mineral complexes are scarce. In this project, a selection of typical PAEs will be used as the model pollutants to explore its interactions with the testing sorbents: natural soil samples, the clay organo-mineral fractions and the simulated organo-mineral complexes to elucidate the mechanisms involved. Based on the characterization of surface and structural properties of these sorbents, the interface behaviors of PAEs on them will be investigated. The correlation of the main characteristic parameters and sorption/desorption coefficients will be established. Specifically, researches will be focused on influencing of the organo-mineral complexes interface interactions affecting biodegradation of PAEs. Theoretical model will be established to describe the relationship between the biodegradability and the sorption/desorption of PAEs by the soils and clay organo-mineral complexes. The biodegradation efficiency of PAEs in different forms in soil will be researched. Moreover, the main factors of soil properties affecting on PAEs biodegradability will also be discussed to understand the mechanism involved contributing to the differences of PAEs biodegradation in agricultural soils. The results will provide scientific basis for the PAEs pollution control and the human health risk management."	
豫西早中三叠世陆相微生物成因构造与遗迹化石的耦合变化	41772110	沉积学和盆地动力学 ( D0206 )	郑伟	副教授	河南理工大学	64.00万元	面上项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2021 年 12 月 31 日	遗迹化石；微生物成因构造；微生物席；早中三叠世；陆地生态系统	Ichnofossils;Microbially Induced Sedimentary Structures;Microbial mat;Early-Middle Triassic;Terrestrial ecosystem	二叠纪末生物大灭绝是显生宙最大的灭绝事件和重大转折期，造就了早中三叠世特殊的生态类群结构、生态格局以及微生物群落的繁盛，使得这一时期的微生物相关的特殊沉积构造以及与后生生物之间相互作用成为关注的焦点和研究前沿。豫西地区下中三叠统发育有丰富的陆相微生物成因构造和遗迹化石，记录了原位的生态特征及古环境信息，为研究早中三叠世陆相生物复苏和古环境制约提供了良好的素材。本项目拟以豫西地区陆相下中三叠统为研究层位，以微生物成因构造和遗迹化石为研究对象，从生物与环境相互作用的角度，将古遗迹学、沉积学与地球微生物学相结合，分析早中三叠世的微生物成因构造与后生动物扰动构造在剖面上的演变规律以及二者之间的耦合变化关系，查明早中三叠世微生物成因构造与遗迹化石及其与环境条件的相互制约关系，为探索早中三叠世陆地生态系统生物复苏方式和机制，以及微生物、后生底栖动物与环境的协同演化提供依据。	"As the greatest biotic catastrophe in the Phanerozoic, the Permian-Triassic mass extinction changed Earth's ecosystems fundamentally. In the aftermath of this crisis, the microbe-dominated ecosystems became prominent and widespread in the Early Triassic. Some unusual biosedimentary structures became a useful sedimentary indication of ecosystem devastation. Abundant microbially induced sedimentary structures and ichnofossils from Lower-Middle Triassic occur in Western Henan Province, and this provide a new material for improving and supplementing the relationship between the biotic recovery and palaeoenvironmental background in the Early-Middle Triassic. Based on the reaction of biological system and environmental factor and study on microbially induced sedimentary structures and ichnofossils from Early-Middle Triassic strata, Western Henan Province, combined with ichnology sedimentology and geobiology methods, this project has three goals: to analysis evolutionary regularity in sections and coupling variation of microbially induced sedimentary structures and ichnofossils; to find out the relationship of microbes and metazoan and its correlation with the environmental conditions in Early-middle Triassic; to supply evidence tempo and mechanisms of terrestrial ecosystem recovery after the Permian-Triassic crisis, and the coevolution between earth's environment and microbes and metazoan."	
基于微生物矿化作用的人为坡面抗侵蚀控制及机理研究	41772280	工程地质环境与灾害 ( D0705 )	唐朝生	教授	南京大学	80.00万元	面上项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2021 年 12 月 31 日	土体工程性质；微观结构；土体侵蚀；边坡稳定性；水土保持	soil engineering property;soil microstructure;soil erosion;slope stability;soil and water preservation	受人类工程地质活动影响，人为坡面的数量和范围趋多趋广，水土流失问题日益严峻，并呈现一系列新的态势，给当前我国水土保持工作带来巨大挑战。本项目以微生物诱导碳酸钙沉积（MICP）作用为技术支撑，以人为坡面为重点研究对象，以提高坡面土体的抗侵蚀性能为研究目的，分别开展室内试验和原位长期观测试验，着重对制约MICP改性土抗侵蚀能力的主要水/力学特性及微观结构特征进行深入研究，阐明MICP改性土的水稳性、抗冲刷性、耐久性及关键因素的影响规律。进一步结合微观分析手段及多学科理论，揭示MICP改性土的抗侵蚀机理。在此基础上，提出一套基于MICP的人为坡面侵蚀生物调控技术和理论，以期使本项目研究成果为水土流失防治提供指导。	"Due to the impact of human engineering geological activities, the number and scale of man-made slopes are becoming more and more extensive, and the problem of soil erosion is becoming more and more serious, and presents a series of new trends, which brings great challenges to the current soil and water conservation work in China. In this project, microbial induced calcite precipitation (MICP) is used as the technical support, and the man-made slope is main study object. The aim of the study is to improve the anti-erosion performance of the slope soil. Both laboratorial experiment and long-term in-situ test will be carried out. The main hydro-mechanical behavior and microstructure characteristics of MICP treated soil will be investigated in detail. The water stability, erosion resistance, and durability of MICP treated soil as well as the related influencing factors will be clarified systematically. Combined with micro-analysis methods and multidisciplinary theory, the anti-erosion mechanism of MICP treated soil will be revealed. On this basis, a set of biological control technology and theory for man-made slope surface erosion based on MICP will be proposed. The research results of project would provide guidance for soil erosion prevention and control."	
玉米-微生物相互作用对玉米吸收累积邻苯二甲酸酯的影响及机理	41773108	环境地球化学 ( D0707 )	蔡全英	教授	暨南大学	68.00万元	面上项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2021 年 12 月 31 日	环境行为；土壤和沉积物；污染物迁移转化	Environmental behavior;Soil and sediment;Contaminant transportation and transformation	邻苯二甲酸酯(PAEs)是一类具有内分泌干扰效应的有机污染物。目前国内外对植物促进微生物降解土壤PAEs等有机污染物研究较多，但关于作物-微生物互作对土壤有机污染物环境过程(尤其是作物吸收累积有机污染物)的影响及机制尚不明确。本项目拟针对我国农田土壤PAEs高风险区，在前期筛选获得PAEs高效降解菌和PAEs低累积玉米品种的基础上，利用盆栽试验和组培实验及批处理方法，采用气相色谱-质谱联机分析和微生物高通量测序技术，研究玉米与微生物互作尤其是根系(及分泌物) 与降解菌(及胞外聚合物)对土壤PAEs的活化/锁定(吸附/解吸)作用，探讨植物酶、根际微生物与降解菌等互作对PAEs的代谢降解及机制，并采用绿色荧光蛋白技术结合激光共聚焦显微镜观察降解菌在玉米根系定殖情况及对玉米累积PAEs影响，从而阐明玉米与微生物互作对玉米吸收累积的影响及机理，为污染土壤生物修复和保障农产品安全提供科学依据。	"Phthalic acid esters (PAEs) are a class of organic contaminants with endocrine disrupting effects. At present, many studies have focused on plant-promoted microbial degradation of organic contaminants (e.g., PAEs) in soil. Nevertheless, the effects of the interaction between plant and microorganism on the environmental process of organic contaminants in soil and its mechanism remain unclear, especially on the uptake and accumulation of organic contaminants by crops. This project will be focused on the high risk area of PAEs in agricultural soil of China. Efficient PAE-degrading strain and low-PAE accumulation cultivar of maize (Zea mays) screened previously by our team will be selected as materials. Series experiments including pot experiments, in vivo plant experiments, and batch experiments will be conducted. The samples of plants, soil and solution will be collected, and PAEs in these samples will be extracted and measured by gas chromatography coupled with mass spectrometry (GC/MS). Microbial communities in rhizospheric and non- rhizospheric soil will be investigated by high-throughput sequencing and quantitative real-time PCR. This project will be aimed to (1) investigate the effects of the interaction between plant and microorganism, especially between plant roots (including its exudates) and PAE-degrading strain (including extracellular polymeric substances), on the activation and sequestration (corresponding sorption and desorption) of PAEs in soil; (2) explore the metabolism and degradation of PAEs by plant enzymes, rhizospheric microorganism, and PAE-degrading strain (including plant endophyte and extracellular polymeric substances) as well as their interaction; (3) observe the colonization of PAE-degrading strain marked with a green fluorescent protein in roots of maize by confocal laser scanning microscopy and investigate its effect on uptake and accumulation of PAEs by maize. All results above will be helpful to elucidate the effects of the interaction between plant and microorganism on uptake and accumulation of PAEs by maize and its mechanism, and will provide scientific basis for bioremediation of soil contaminated by organic contaminants and for the safety of agricultural products."	
土壤-地下水环境微生物群落对铬迁移转化的影响机制和模型研究	41773111	环境地球化学 ( D0707 )	刘媛媛	副教授	南京大学	68.00万元	面上项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2021 年 12 月 31 日	重金属；迁移转化；环境地球化学过程；微生物群落	Heavy metal;Reactive transport;Biogeochemical processes;Microbial community	铬是土壤和地下水中重点防控的重金属污染物。土壤-地下水生态系统对铬具有阻滞并降低其毒性的功能，这种功能与微生物驱动的氧、碳、氮、铁、锰、硫等关键元素的生物地球化学过程显著相关，因而研究这一多元素过程并揭示微生物群落在其中的作用是理解土壤-地下水生态系统对铬阻滞和转化功能的关键。本项目通过实验与数值模拟相结合的方法，探明关键元素循环对铬迁移转化过程的影响机制，揭示微生物群落结构和功能对铬和关键元素生物地球化学过程的响应、反馈、调控机制，并进一步建立耦合了微生物群落功能的反应-运移模型，模拟铬在土壤和地下水中的迁移转化行为。该模型具有示范作用，可展示土壤-地下水生态系统对氧化-还原敏感污染物的转化功能，为污染物诊断和风险评价提供量化工具，为土壤和地下水原位修复提供理论支撑。	"Cr is a common redox sensitive metal contaminant in the soil and groundwater. The soil-groundwater ecosystem plays an important role on immobilization, retardation, and detoxification of Cr. Such role is significantly influenced by the biogeochemical cycling of O, C, N, Fe, Mn, and S driven by microbial activity. Understanding the influence of microbial activity on element cycling and reactive transport of Cr is the key to reveal the role of soil-groundwater ecosystem. This proposed study is to investigate the coupled element cycling and reactive transport of Cr; to reveal how the coupled biogeochemical processes affect the microbial community structure and its functional potential, which in turn regulates the pathways and rates of the biogeochemical processes; and to establish a reactive transport model that integrates the dynamic role of microbial community. The integrated model is able to simulate reactive transport of Cr in the soil and groundwater. This study can be used as an example to illustrate the role of the soil-groundwater ecosystem on migration and transformation of redox sensitive contaminants. Such role is important for risk assessment of soil and groundwater contaminants and development of in-situ remediation technologies."	
基于hgcAB同源基因探针研究大九湖湿地汞微生物甲基化作用机制	41773112	环境地球化学 ( D0707 )	刘金铃	副教授	中国地质大学（武汉）	68.00万元	面上项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2021 年 12 月 31 日	甲基汞；汞甲基化；湿地；微生物	Methylmercury;Mercury methylation;Wetland;Microorganism	湿地是一类汞敏感性生态系统。经大气沉降进入湿地的汞更易甲基化产生毒性更高的甲基汞，经食物链富集在高营养级生物，威胁生态系统的稳定性和生物多样性。然而，大气沉降汞源为主的湿地中汞甲基化机理尚未明确。本项目以典型雨养型湿地――大九湖为研究对象，利用hgcAB同源基因探针结合宏基因组学手段，弄清沉积物中甲基化微生物群落特征；采用微生物培养和汞稳定同位素示踪技术，判别介导汞甲基化的关键微生物类群；结合野外和室内模拟试验研究汞的地球化学形态、微生物可利用性及影响因素，明确影响湿地沉积物汞甲基化的主要因子。通过本研究，最终弄清以大气汞源为主的大九湖湿地中汞微生物甲基化过程及机理，为全面认识汞的生物地球化学循环提供研究基础，并为有效控制湿地甲基汞的产生，减少汞危害，保护水源地和生态系统提供理论依据。	"Wetland is a mercury-sensitive ecosystem. Mercury (Hg) that enters into wetland via atmospheric deposition is easily methylated to methylmercury (MeHg) which is more toxic. MeHg could be accumulated in biota at trophic level through food chain, threatening the stability and biodiversity of ecosystem. However, the mechanism of Hg methylation in the wetland where Hg is mainly from atmospheric deposition is still unclear. This project will focus on the mechanism of Hg methylated by microbes in a typical peatland―Dajiu lake. To begin with, the hgcAB orthologues probe and metagenomics methods will be applied to investigate methylating microbial communities and features. Besides, the techniques of microculture in lab and Hg stable isotope tracer will be used to identify the key microbes mediating Hg methylation. Moreover, both field studies and lab tests will be designed to investigate geochemical forms of Hg, Hg availability for microorganisms, and impact environmental factors. Finally, the process and mechanism of Hg methylation in Dajiuhu wetland will be clarified. This project will be fundamental for reaching an overview of the biogeochemical cycle of Hg, and providing a basis of how to control MeHg production, to reduce the hazard, and to protect water sources and the ecosystem."	
基于iChip技术的海洋“未培养”微生物资源挖掘及新天然产物发现	41776168	生物海洋学与海洋生物资源 ( D0604 )	何山	副教授	宁波大学	64.00万元	面上项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2021 年 12 月 31 日	海洋微生物；未培养；分离芯片；分子网络；天然产物	marine microbes;uncultured;iChip;molecular networking;natural products	海洋独特的生态环境孕育了海洋微生物复杂的生命机制，占海洋微生物资源99％以上的“未培养”类群因无法用传统技术培养而未被有效利用，是具有巨大潜在应用前景的新资源。科学证据表明，绝大多数微生物的生长依赖于特定生境以及微生物种群之间的群体感应与化学交流，因此，“原位培养”是获得“未培养”微生物的关键。本项目拟运用高通量原位培养新技术iChip，以红树林沉积物、近海沉积物、海水等作为研究对象，原位培养获得多样性丰富的海洋“未培养”微生物新资源，通过多相分类法鉴定若干新分类单元。运用分子网络技术研究其次级代谢产物的化学多样性与独特性，结合现代色谱和波谱方法，发现具有新颖化学结构的天然产物。并进一步开展体外抗菌、抗肿瘤、抗阿尔兹海默病活性筛选，获得高活性化合物。本项目的实施将为挖掘利用海洋“未培养”微生物新资源开辟一条有效途径，为我国海洋创新药物研发提供新的对象。	"The marine special ecological environment has led to complex life mechanism of marine microbes. However, more than 99% of marine microbial resource still can’t be cultured by traditional cultivation technique. Marine uncultured microbes are therefore new resource with huge application potential. Scientific evidence showed that most microbes need special environment and chemical communication among them to grow. Therefore, in situ cultivation is the key to access uncultured microbes. This project plans to use new high-throughput in situ cultivation technique iChip to cultivate marine uncultured microbes with rich biodiversity from mangrove sediment, nearshore sediment, and sea water. Polyphasic approach is employed to characterize new taxa. Their secondary metabolites are analyzed by molecular networking technology to investigate their chemodiversity and uniqueness. We expect to discover structurally novel compounds by modern chromatographic and spectroscopic means. The new natural products will be screened by antibacterial, antitumor, and anti-Alzheimer’s disease models to discover potent compounds. This project will pave a new way for exploiting marine uncultured microbial new resources, and to provide candidates for marine new drug discovery in our country."	
南海暗光层颗粒有机物附着微生物的组成和潜在生态功能研究	41776147	生物海洋学与海洋生物资源 ( D0604 )	荆红梅	研究员	中国科学院深海科学与工程研究所	66.00万元	面上项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2021 年 12 月 31 日	南中国海；暗光层；颗粒有机物动态；微生物群落结构；代谢功能	South China Sea;Twilight zone;POM dynamics;Microbial community structure;Metabolic function	颗粒有机碳(POC)从表面到深海的输运是碳汇的重要机制，它可以降低大气中CO2的浓度。 POC垂直输出通量随深度在海洋中层或“暗光层”迅速衰减，其中微生物和浮游动物降解和消费下沉的POC来支持他们的代谢需求。海洋暗光层发生的颗粒有机物(POM)的分解、聚合、矿化等过程，决定着真光层中的颗粒有机物向深海中的沉降和海洋生物泵的效率。但目前相关研究还集中在颗粒有机物本身的动力学变化，而缺乏参与这些过程的微生物的群落结构和代谢功能信息。本项目计划从我国南海深海盆区入手，针对夏季和冬季在真光层(50m)，暗光层的上层(150m)和下层(800m)处所采集到的不同粒径的颗粒有机物，分析其在沉降过程中的组分变化，并利用宏基因组和宏转录组研究其附着微生物群落的结构组成和参与碳、氮等循环的主要代谢途径，探讨微生物在暗光层不同粒径颗粒有机物的动态变化中的潜在功能和对调控南海暗光层有机碳通量的贡献。	"Transport of particulate organic carbon (POC) from the surface to the deep ocean is an important mechanism of carbon sequestration that could lower the concentration of atmospheric CO2. The vertical POC flux attenuates rapidly with depth in the ocean’s mesopelagic or “twilight” zone (depths immediately below the euphotic zone down to about 1,000m), where microbes and zooplankton solubilize and consume sinking particulate organic matter (POM) to support their metabolic demands. However, little is known about the microbes that are involved in these complex degradation processes, which determines the proportion of POC flux from the euphotic zone to the deep ocean, i.e., the efficiency of biological pump. We plan to conduct a metagenomic and metatranscriptomic study on the microbial communities associated in particles in the deep basin of the South China Sea to elucidate their composition and metabolism in the particle degradation processes in the twilight zone. Organic particles of three different sizes will be collected from the euphotic zone (50m) and the upper boundary (150m) and lower boundary (800m) of the twilight zone in both summer and winter. Chemical properties of the particles will be characterized and the community composition and metabolic functions of microbes that are related to POM remineralization will be revealed from bioinformatics analysis of the metagenomic and metatranscriptomic data. Information generated from this project will help to evaluate the microbial roles in controlling the dynamics of export flux of POC in the twilight zone in the South China Sea."	
双氰胺对北方棕壤土壤微生物代谢α-酮戊二酸的影响	41701300	土壤生物学 ( D070104 )	王振宇	讲师	辽宁科技学院	25.00万元	青年科学基金项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2020 年 12 月 31 日	双氰胺；土壤微生物；北方棕壤；α-酮戊二酸；代谢	Dicyandiamide;soil microbe;brown soil in northern China;α-ketoglutaric acid;metabolism	双氰胺（Dicyandiamide，DCD）是一种被广泛应用的硝化抑制剂，其可以延长土壤硝化作用，减少氮素的损失，提高氮肥的利用率。目前，常采用定量土壤氨氧化基因丰度的方法，评估硝化抑制剂的施用效果和生态学风险，而从微生物群落代谢功能角度来评估硝化抑制剂对环境影响的研究工作鲜有报道。本课题组前期研究发现，在室内模拟实验和田间实验中，DCD均可使土壤分解α-酮戊二酸的潜力显著降低，推测这是土壤微生物群落氮循环受到人为干预后作出的响应。本项目拟将北方棕壤作为研究对象，研究DCD对土壤微生物群落代谢功能的影响机制。项目采用Microresp和实时定量PCR技术，判断受到DCD扰动较大的碳代谢节点；采用离子色谱技术研究α-酮戊二酸等低分子量有机酸的微生物群落代谢特征，旨在研究土壤微生物群落代谢功能在生理和基因水平上对DCD干扰的响应机制，为全面评估DCD的施用效果和风险提供理论依据。	"Dicyandiamide is a worldwide used nitrification inhibitor. It could prolong the nitrification, reduce the nitrogen loss, enhance the nitrogen efficiency. Now, assessments of the genes abundances of ammonia monooxygenase are often used to evaluate the effects of nitrification inhibitors on ecological risk and economic efficiency, but there were few assessments of nitrification inhibitors on microbes’ community level physiological profile in soil. Our preliminary research findings showed that metabolism potentials of α-ketoglutaric acid in brown soil were reduced significantly by the application of DCD in both microcosm study and field study, which speculated this phenomenon was the consequence of soil microbe community to application of DCD in soil. In this project, brown soil in northern China will be studied to investigate the soil microbial community metabolism mechanism under DCD treatment. In this project, ion chromatography, MicrorespTM and real-time PCR were used to evaluate the nodes of carbon metabolism which were sensitive to DCD and investigate the α-ketoglutaric acid (as well as other low molecular organic acids) metabolic features in the soil microbial community. After the application of DCD, the soil microbial community metabolic functions in physiological and genetic levels were analyzed to provide support for comprehensively evaluating the ecological risk and economic efficiency."	
水稻田微生物催化的铁还原型甲烷厌氧氧化过程及其机理研究	41701274	土壤生物学 ( D070104 )	何崭飞	讲师	浙江工业大学	26.00万元	青年科学基金项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2020 年 12 月 31 日	甲烷厌氧氧化；铁还原；水稻土；富集培养；微生物机理	anaerobic oxidation of methane (AOM);iron reduction;paddy soil;enrichment culture;microbial mechanism	近年来，在微生物甲烷厌氧氧化领域获得了两项重大突破，其一是揭示了甲烷厌氧氧化古菌与硫酸盐还原细菌之间的电子传递方式，其二是实验室证实了铁还原型甲烷厌氧氧化（Fe-AOM）过程。目前零星的研究表明，Fe-AOM过程可能存在于包括水稻土在内的许多生境中，Fe-AOM过程可能由古菌单独或古菌与细菌协作完成，但由于至今未获得“真正”的富集物，Fe-AOM过程机理尚不明确。本项目拟采用同位素示踪、高通量测序等技术，调查Fe-AOM微生物在水稻田中的分布特征，并以高Fe-AOM活性的水稻土为接种物，富集培养Fe-AOM微生物；采用光谱分析、高通量测序等技术，对富集物进行物理、化学、生物特性表征；以Fe-AOM富集物为实验材料，采用同位素示踪、宏基因组测序等技术，揭示Fe-AOM过程的代谢途径和电子传递方式。该项研究不仅能丰富人们对Fe-AOM过程的认识，还能为水稻田甲烷减排提供更多思路。	"Recently, two great breakthroughs have been made in the field of anaerobic oxidation of methane: first, the mechanisms of extracellular electron transfer between anaerobic methanotrophic archaea and sulfate-reducing bacteria were revealed; second, the bioprocess of iron-dependent anaerobic oxidation of methane (Fe-AOM) was finally confirmed by laboratory evidences. At present, some sporadic studies suggest that Fe-AOM may occur in many natural habitats, such as paddy soil, and may be mediated by archaea or by archaea and bacteria together. However, due to the lack of the “true” Fe-AOM culture, microbial mechanisms of Fe-AOM, including microbial metabolism and extracellular electron transfer between microorganisms and iron minerals, remain unclear. In this project, using isotope tracer and high-throughput sequencing, the distribution of Fe-AOM microorganisms in paddy will be investigated; the paddy soil with the highest Fe-AOM activity will be collected as inoculum to enrich and cultivate Fe-AOM microorganisms. Using spectrum analysis and high-throughput sequencing, the physical, chemical and biological features of the Fe-AOM culture will be characterized; substrate affinity, substrate diversity and the response to environmental factors of Fe-AOM microorganisms will also be investigated. Using isotope tracer and metagenomic sequencing, the metabolic pathway and extracellular electron transfer of Fe-AOM microorganisms will be revealed. The results of this project will not only enrich our knowledge of Fe-AOM process, but also provide more ideas for reducing methane emission from paddy fields."	
废水生物处理过程中微生物胞外抗性基因的存在及水平转移机制	51708533	污水处理与资源化 ( E080402 )	袁丽	博士后	中国科学技术大学	26.00万元	青年科学基金项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2020 年 12 月 31 日	基因水平转移；活性污泥；城市污水处理厂；胞外抗生素抗性基因；抗生素	Horizontal gene transfer;Activated sludge;Municipal wastewater treatment plant;Extracellular antibiotic resistance genes;Antibiotics	环境中抗生素抗性基因（ARGs）的存在形态包括胞内ARGs和胞外ARGs，胞外ARGs在一定条件下可持久性存在并发生水平转移，但因为胞外DNA提取难度较大，目前有关胞外ARGs的研究仍然很少。针对城市污水厂是环境ARGs的重要污染源，且含有大量胞外DNA，本项目拟系统开展活性污泥胞外ARGs分布及水平转移研究。首先拟建立活性污泥胞外DNA的提纯方法，明确污水厂不同处理单元中胞外ARGs的存在水平，揭示其在污水厂中的归趋。在实验室条件下，考察抗生素存在与否时，反应器工艺参数对活性污泥胞外ARGs丰度的影响，识别关键影响工艺参数；在此基础上，探明外源胞外ARGs的持久性和水平转移潜力，同时分析活性污泥微生物群落结构和胞内ARGs、可遗传元件整合子的丰度，建立胞外ARGs与微生物群落结构、胞内ARGs、整合子的内在联系。该研究对于揭示胞外ARGs在废水生物处理过程中的传播扩散规律具有指导意义。	"Environmental antibiotic resistance genes (ARGs) consist of both intracellular (iARGs) and extracellular ARGs (eARGs). The eARGs are likely more persistent and can spread via horizontal gene transfer under certain environmental conditions. However, up to date, very little is known about eARGs due to the difficulty in extraction and purification of extracellular DNA (eDNA). Considering that municipal wastewater treatment plants (MWTPs) are important sources of environmental ARGs with high content of eDNA in activated sludge, this work aims to investigate the occurrence and gene transfer of eARGs in the activated sludge process. First, a reliable method for extraction and purification of eDNA in activated sludge is developed for exploring the distribution and abundance of eARGs in different treatment units of MWTPs, aiming to reveal the fate of eARGs in MWTPs. In laboratory conditions, the effects of bioreactor operation parameters on the eARGs abundance in the presence and absence of antibiotic selection pressure are determined, and the key operation parameters are also identified. Thereafter, we study the persistence and gene transfer potential of exogenous eARGs as well as determine the microbial composition of activated sludge and the abundance of iARGs and integron. The internal relation between eARGs and microbial composition, iARGs, and integron is built based on above results. This research will provide helpful information for revealing the gene transfer mechanism of eARGs in wastewater biological treatment system."	
低温条件下全程自养脱氮工艺的磁场强化及其微生物响应机理研究	51708263	污水处理与资源化 ( E080402 )	贾文林	讲师	江苏师范大学	25.00万元	青年科学基金项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2020 年 12 月 31 日	全程自养脱氮工艺；磁场强化；低温；微生物响应机理；生物脱氮	Completely autotrophic nitrogen removal over nitrite process;Magnetic field intensified;Low temperature;Microbial response;Biological nitrogen removal	全程自养脱氮工艺（CANON）被认为是最经济便捷的污水生物脱氮路径之一，然而，该工艺在低温条件下存在启动周期长、脱氮效率低、运行不稳定等问题，限制了其工程化应用。而该工艺中不同自养微生物生长代谢特征的差异，导致低温下该工艺的强化比较困难。为解决以上问题，本项目通过向CANON工艺施加适宜的磁场，并优化磁场产生和作用方式，以强化该工艺在低温条件下的脱氮效率和运行稳定性；分析磁场作用下CANON工艺反应器内活性污泥结构、微生物形态及群落结构的变化，明确该工艺相关自养脱氮微生物对磁场强化作用的响应特征；研究磁场作用下相关微生物主要功能酶活性及微生物自我调控信号分子的变化，结合微生物胞外物质组成及反应器内物质转化过程，解析磁场作用下微生物的响应机理；并根据以上研究，建立磁场强化型CANON污水处理系统并处理实际污水，评价其运行效果。本研究成果将为CANON工艺的工程化应用提供理论和技术支持	"Completely autotrophic nitrogen removal over nitrite process (CANON) is considered as one of the most efficient biological nitrogen removal processes. However, the application of CANON process is limited due to the long startup period as well as low and fluctuant nitrogen removal efficiency at low temperature. Moreover, the metabolic characteristics of autotrophic microorganisms employed in CANON process are varied, which is unfavorable for the enhancement of CANON process at low temperature. In order to solve the above problems, the CANON process will be exposed to magnetic field in the proposed project, and the operation of magnetic field will be optimized to enhance the nitrogen removal efficiency and running stability of CANON process. The morphology of activated sludge and the structure of microbial communities will be measured to determine the response characteristics of microorganisms to the magnetic field at low temperature. Meanwhile, the variations of related enzyme activities and signal molecules release in the microorganisms will be detected, and the components of extracellular polymeric substance secreted by microorganisms will also be analyzed. Combined with the transformation of nitrogen in reactors, the microbial response mechanisms to magnetic field will be further explored. Based on the above research, the intensified CANON process by magnetic field will be established and used to treat actual wastewater and the performance will be evaluated. The successful completion of the proposed project will provide theoretical and technical support for the application of CANON process."	
“微生物固化加筋垫层-刚性桩”路基结构承载性能与变形控制特性	51708243	地基与基础工程 ( E080601 )	赖汉江	博士后	华中科技大学	26.00万元	青年科学基金项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2020 年 12 月 31 日	地基处理；桩承式加筋路堤；微生物固化；加筋垫层；变形控制	ground improvement;geogrid-reinforced and pile-supported embankment;microbially induced calcite precipitation;reinforced cushion;deformation control	针对桩板式路基结构价格昂贵和传统桩承式加筋路堤变形控制效果不佳等问题，本项目旨在研发一种环境友好的“微生物固化纤维-格栅加筋垫层-刚性桩”（Bio-FGR-RP）路基结构，达到经济高效地控制路基变形的目的。该新型路基结构涉及极为复杂的多元耦联作用，其承载性能和变形控制特性尚不明确。本项目将开展系列宏细观试验，明确微生物固化纤维加筋砂土（Bio-FS）的工程力学特性，优化纤维加筋及微生物固化参数，建立Bio-FS材料本构模型；然后基于抗弯强度试验及数值模拟，全面揭示微生物固化纤维-格栅加筋（Bio-FGR）垫层性能演化规律及各部分协同工作机制；最后通过室内模型试验及数值建模，深入探究Bio-FGR-RP路基结构的荷载传递机理与变形控制特性，凝练实用的Bio-FGR-RP路基设计理论。项目研究成果将为软土地区路基处理提供新途径，为Bio-FGR-RP路基结构的全面推广与应用奠定理论及试验基础。	"In view of the problem that the expensive pile-plate subgrade structure and the imperfect deformation control effect in the traditional geogrid-reinforced and pile-supported embankment, this project aims to develop an environmentally friendly subgrade structure consisting of Bio-cemented Fiber-Geogrid Reinforced cushion and Rigid Piles (termed as Bio-FGR-RP subgrade structure) to economically and efficiently control the deformation of subgrade. However, the load-transfer and deformation controlling characteristics of the Bio-FGR-RP subgrade structure are unclear due to the extremely complex multiple coupling effect involved in this new subgrade structure. A series of experimental tests in macro and micro perspectives will be conducted in this project to investigate the engineering mechanical properties of Bio-cemented Fiber Sand (Bio-FS), optimize the parameters regarding to fiber and microbial induced calcite precipitation and establish the material constitutive model of Bio-FS. Afterwards, the bending strength tests and numerical simulations will be carried out to reveal the performance evolution and the coordination working mechanisms of all the parts of Bio-cemented Fiber-Geogrid Reinforced (Bio-FGR) cushion. Finally, the laboratory model experiments and numerical simulations will also be conducted to deeply investigate the load transfer mechanism and deformation controlling characteristics of Bio-FGR-RP subgrade structure and refine the useful design theory of the Bio-FGR-RP subgrade structure. The research findings of this project will give new ways for subgrade treatment in soft soil area, and meanwhile, establish theoretical and experimental supports for the comprehensive popularization and application of this new subgrade structure in actual engineering."	
基于宏基因组测序数据的微生物基因组序列鉴定及群落比较方法研究	11701546	生物数学 ( A011403 )	宋凯	助理研究员	中国科学院海洋研究所	24.00万元	青年科学基金项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2020 年 12 月 31 日	宏基因组学；相似性分析	metagenomics;similarity analysis	人体中的微生物群落与人体的健康息息相关，有研究表明几十种疾病都与人体微生物群落的失调有关系。随着二代测序技术迅猛发展并且在宏基因组学的研究中发挥了越来越重要的作用，令深入探索微生物群落的组成与相互关系成为了可能。然而微生物群落是一个多种微生物混合的复杂体，如何利用宏基因组测序数据鉴定每种微生物的基因组序列及相对丰度等信息，并将其应用于微生物群落的相互比较是一个重要的课题。本项目将致力于开发宏基因组测序数据分析与比较的统计模型与方法，着重解决下面问题：（1）开发微生物基因组序列及相对丰度推断的概率统计方法，（2）开发微生物群落相似性度量的新统计量，（3）整合不同的微生物群落比较方法。本项目将为微生物群落的生物信息学领域提供新的研究方法，并推进我们对微生物群落与人体健康之间关系的理解。	"The microbial community in the human body is closely related to the health of the human body. Some studies have shown that dozens of diseases are related to the maladjustment of human microbial community. With the rapid development of the next generation sequencing technology which played an important role in the research of metagenomics, it is possible to explore the relationship between microbial community composition, interrelationships and environmental variables. However, the microbial community is a complex of multiple microorganisms. How to use the genome sequencing data to identify the genome sequence and relative abundance of each microorganism and apply it to the understanding and comparison of microbial community is an important subject. The project will focus on the development of the statistical models and methods in the area of metagenomics data analysis and comparison. It focuses on solving the following questions: (1) developing the probability and statistical methods for identifying microbial genome sequences and estimating the relative abundance, (2) developing a new statistic for microbial community similarity measures, (3) integrating different microbial community comparison methods. The project will provide new bioinformatical methods for the research of microbial communities and advance our understanding of the relationship between microbial communities and human health."	
生物海绵铁体系中铁与微生物协同同步反硝化作用机制及其应用基础研究	51768032	污水处理与资源化 ( E080402 )	王亚娥	教授	兰州交通大学	40.00万元	地区科学基金项目	2018 年 01 月 01 日 至 2021 年 12 月 31 日	污水处理；生物海绵铁；脱氮机理；同步反硝化	wastewater treatment;biological sponge iron;denitrification mechanism;simultaneous denitrification	"随着经济高速发展及城镇化进程的不断加快，氮素造成的水体污染日趋严重，加大污水脱氮力度，严格控制氮排放，已成为环保工作面临的重要任务。开发操作简便、经济高效的实用新型脱氮工艺已成为研究的热点。前期研究发现，好氧条件下生物海绵铁体系(Biological Sponge Iron System,简称BSIS)具有良好脱氮效果，但脱氮作用机理尚不清楚。本课题拟以间歇式BSIS为对象，通过考察体系中海绵铁表面生物膜内的缺氧同步反硝化特征与体系中铁对硝化及反硝化菌群多样性影响，揭示该体系中铁与微生物协同作用下的同步反硝化作用机制，为开发新型高效脱氮工艺提供理论基础。研究内容包括: BSIS强化脱氮效果及其影响因素研究；BSIS中缺氧反硝化特征研究；BSIS中铁对硝化及反硝化菌群多样性影响研究；BSIS中好氧反硝化菌的富集、分离纯化与脱氮性能研究；BSIS中强化硝化与同步好氧反硝化技术研究。"	"With the high-speed development of economy and the accelerating of urbanization process, nitrogen pollution of water body has become increasingly serious. The most important mission for the cultural working of environmental protection was to increase the intensity of sewage denitrification and strictly control the emissions of nitrogen. The study carried out new denitrogenation process which simplifies the operation, reduces production cost is being studied intensively. Previous studies have found that biological sponge iron system(BSIS) has strong denitrification effect in aerobic conditions, but the denitrification mechanism was unclear. In the present project, its mechanism of simultaneous denitrification under the synergistic effect of iron and microbiology will be revealed by studying the characteristics of anoxic denitrification inside biofilm attaching on the surface of sponge iron and the impact of iron on diversity of nitrifying bacteria and denitrifying bacteria using Sequencing Batch Reactor(SBR) with biological sponge iron and can provide theory foundation for developing new type denitrogenation process.The main contents of the project include：(1)The effect and affecting factors of denitrogenation in the BSIS. (2)the characteristics of anoxic denitrification in the BSIS. (3)The impact of iron on diversity of nitrifying bacteria and denitrifying bacteria in the BSIS. (4)The enrichment, separation, depuration and denitrification performance of aerobic denitrifying bacteria in the BSIS.(5)The enhancement techniques of nitrification and simultaneous aerobic denitrification in the BSIS."
